Qi'ra apologized while Vos said that Qi'ra was loyal to Crimson Dawn. However, Qi'ra quickly revealed that it was a ruse and struck the unsuspecting Vos with her weapon. Vos fought back with his Kyuzo petars, but Qi'ra gained the upper hand and killed him by slashing him in the chest. Qi'ra told Han to go after Chewbacca and Beckett, telling him that if they gave their coaxium to Enfys, they would need something else to buy a new ship. Before parting company, Qi'ra embraced Han and reminded him to look after Chewbacca and to smile. She told him that she would be right behind him.[[9]](#cite_note-Solo-9)

 [![Solo and Chewbacca watch Qi'ra leave Savareen.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/HanChewbaccaWatchFirstLightDeparture-Solo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181014195608) [![Solo and Chewbacca watch Qi'ra leave Savareen.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/HanChewbaccaWatchFirstLightDeparture-Solo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20181014195608)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/HanChewbaccaWatchFirstLightDeparture-Solo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181014195608) 

Solo and Chewbacca watch Qi'ra leave Savareen.

 

After Han left, Qi'ra removed Dryden Vos' signet ring and used it to seal the living room. Alone aboard Vos' yacht, Qi'ra contacted Vos' superior, the former Sith apprentice Maul. She informed him of the coaxium mission's failure and assumed Vos' position but carefully avoided telling him about Han's involvement, instead pinning the blame on Beckett. Using the Force to draw his dagger, Maul ordered Qi'ra to bring the yacht to the planet Dathomir and told her that together they would deal with the traitors, before stating that she would be working more closely with him in the future.[[9]](#cite_note-Solo-9)

##### Choosing allegiances[]

Meanwhile, Han caught up with Beckett and Chewbacca along the Pnakotic Coast. Beckett said that Han was relentless while Han told Chewie that he came as fast as he could. Han confirmed that Dryden was dead and that Qi'ra killed him. Beckett said that Han still didn't understand that Qi'ra was a survivor. Han responded that Beckett's problem was that he thought that everyone was like him. Beckett responded that Han was not like him. He tried to trick Han into lowering his guard by offering to tell something while reaching for his blaster.[[9]](#cite_note-Solo-9)

Before Beckett could shoot him, Han shot first, fatally wounding the gangster. Han helped up the dying Beckett who complimented Han for his quick thinking, admitting that he would have killed him had Han not reacted. Beckett praised Han for his courage on the Vandor mountain before breathing his last. Han watched as Qi'ra departed on the yacht First Light, having given Solo a clean break from his debts to the Crimson Dawn. Qi'ra watched Han and Chewbacca from the viewport. Chewie put a comforting hand on Han.[[9]](#cite_note-Solo-9)

Following the deaths of Vos and Beckett, Han and Chewbacca delivered the refined coaxium to Nest, who revealed her plans to use the coaxium, which was worth 60 million credits, to aid the rebellion against the Empire. She offered Han the chance to join her, but he declined. In response, Nest stated that someday he might feel more sympathetic to the rebels' cause. Out of gratitude for his help, Nest gave Solo a vial of coaxium, enough to buy a ship for himself.[[9]](#cite_note-Solo-9)

##### Further adventures[]

:   "*You thinking what I'm thinking?*"
:   ―Solo to Chewbacca on Savareen[[32]](#cite_note-Solo_Comic_7-32)

Following their departure from Savareen, Chewie and Solo paired up on various jobs, including one where they were riding a [74-Z speeder bike](/wiki/74-Z_speeder_bike "74-Z speeder bike") under fire and another where Solo was tied up. Eventually, they found their way to [Numidian Prime](/wiki/Numidian_Prime "Numidian Prime").[[32]](#cite_note-Solo_Comic_7-32)

##### Winning the *Falcon*[]

:   "*Fair and square, baby. Fair and square.*"
:   ―Han Solo[[9]](#cite_note-Solo-9)

 [![Han used his coaxium as a buy-in to play sabacc with Lando and win the Millennium Falcon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/CoaxiumHyperfuel-SWZ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190810011449) [![Han used his coaxium as a buy-in to play sabacc with Lando and win the Millennium Falcon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/CoaxiumHyperfuel-SWZ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190810011449)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/CoaxiumHyperfuel-SWZ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190810011449) 

Han used his coaxium as a buy-in to play sabacc with Lando and win the *Millennium Falcon*.

 

Elsewhere, Han and Chewbacca soon tracked down Lando to a jungle outpost on Numidian Prime, where Lando was regaling patrons about his adventures in StarCave Nebula. Han chided Lando for leaving them on Savareen before embracing him. When Lando asked for his cut, Han replied he was not getting any since they barely survived their last adventure. After exchanging pleasantries, Han again challenged Lando to a sabacc game for possession of the *Falcon*. Han had previously subtly relieved Lando of the cards stashed up his sleeve and therefore won the game.[[9]](#cite_note-Solo-9)

After acquiring the *Falcon*, Han told Chewbacca that he planned to go to Tatooine, where Beckett told him that a gangster was putting together an organization. The Falcon then jumped into hyperspace.[[9]](#cite_note-Solo-9)

#### Captain of the *Millennium Falcon*[]

##### New adventures[]

 [![Han and Chewie in the cockpit of their newly acquired Millennium Falcon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Winners_of_the_Falcon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181019051828) [![Han and Chewie in the cockpit of their newly acquired Millennium Falcon](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Winners_of_the_Falcon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181019051828)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Winners_of_the_Falcon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181019051828) 

Han and Chewie in the cockpit of their newly acquired *Millennium Falcon*

 

The *Falcon* instantly became Solo's most prized possession. With their newly acquired ship and confidence, Solo and Chewbacca began engaging in much more dangerous and risky criminal operations, eventually becoming smugglers.[[33]](#cite_note-Ultimate-33) Around the same time, Chewbacca hung Han's pair of [chance cubes](/wiki/Chance_cube "Chance cube") above the freighter's piloting console.[[34]](#cite_note-Smuggler's_Run-34) At some point during their travels, the two met [Dash Rendar](/wiki/Dash_Rendar "Dash Rendar").[[23]](#cite_note-TFV-23)

Solo and Chewbacca also became acquainted with the infamous [Tonnika sisters](/wiki/Tonnika_sisters "Tonnika sisters"), but the many events that occurred between both parties left their relationship soured.[[35]](#cite_note-You_Owe_Me_a_Ride-35) On one occasion, Solo and Calrissian attended a party aboard a [casino](/wiki/Casino "Casino") starship, aboard which they met up with the sisters, on the [Hydian Way](/wiki/Hydian_Way "Hydian Way").[[36]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-36) One event—remembered by the sisters as the "[Lando ordeal](/wiki/Lando_ordeal "Lando ordeal")"—was Solo's idea, but he blamed them for what happened.[[35]](#cite_note-You_Owe_Me_a_Ride-35) Calrissian's business partner [Lobot](/wiki/Lobot "Lobot") also became familiar with Solo.[[37]](#cite_note-The_Angle-37)

##### Chewie's day off[]

:   "*Tell you what. You need a break.*"
:   ―Han Solo, to Chewbacca[[38]](#cite_note-Chewie's_Day_Off-38)

Solo piloted the *Falcon* through an asteroid field during a run to sell marked sabacc decks to the [casino](/wiki/Unidentified_resort_casino "Unidentified resort casino") on [Marquinn](/wiki/Marquinn "Marquinn"). He told Chewbacca to take the day off while he sold marked sabacc decks to the casino's owner [Zefin Tuzo](/wiki/Zefin_Tuzo "Zefin Tuzo"). During Chewbacca's day off, he countered a criminal named [Vullen Candroon](/wiki/Vullen_Candroon "Vullen Candroon") which wanted to kill Chewbacca. Chewbacca escaped Candroon but ran into Zefin Tuzo, who was working with Vullen. Later, Chewbacca managed to escape Candroon and Tuzo. Meanwhile Han was talking to patrons in the casino. Chewbacca immediately ran into the casino to get Han because he was getting chased by Candroon and Tuzo. Later, Han and Chewbacca managed to escape aboard the *Millennium Falcon*.[[38]](#cite_note-Chewie's_Day_Off-38)

##### Chased by Kallus[]

:   "*You've made quite a name for yourself.*"
:   ―Alexsandr Kallus to Han Solo[[39]](#cite_note-Flight_of_the_Falcon_1-39)

 [![Solo confronted by ISB Agent Kallus](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/KallusSolo-SpyGames.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181013023121) [![Solo confronted by ISB Agent Kallus](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/KallusSolo-SpyGames.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/258?cb=20181013023121)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/KallusSolo-SpyGames.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181013023121) 

Solo confronted by ISB Agent Kallus

 

[Imperial Security Bureau](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") agent [Alexsandr Kallus](/wiki/Alexsandr_Kallus "Alexsandr Kallus") hired the bounty hunter [IG-88](/wiki/IG-88B "IG-88B") to assist in tracking down Solo, with the intention of bringing the smuggler to justice for defecting from the Empire and assisting Enfys Nest. Solo and Chewbacca fled the two, and escaped capture by flying the *Falcon* between two Imperial Star Destroyers.[[39]](#cite_note-Flight_of_the_Falcon_1-39)

##### The Cordaxian Sea[]

:   "*Kill you...kill you both for this...*"
:   ―Frax to Han Solo[[40]](#cite_note-Annual_3-40)

 [![Frax points his gun at Han Solo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/FraxPointsGunAtHan-2015StarWarsAnnual3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181014174953) [![Frax points his gun at Han Solo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/FraxPointsGunAtHan-2015StarWarsAnnual3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/209?cb=20181014174953)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/FraxPointsGunAtHan-2015StarWarsAnnual3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181014174953) 

Frax points his gun at Han Solo.

 

Some time after escaping Kallus,[[39]](#cite_note-Flight_of_the_Falcon_1-39) Solo and Chewbacca were transporting two tons of [Cordaxian ore](/wiki/Cordaxian_ore "Cordaxian ore") on the planet [Odona](/wiki/Odona "Odona"), with the help of [Frax](/wiki/Frax "Frax"), a [Kajain'sa'Nikto](/wiki/Kajain%27sa%27Nikto "Kajain'sa'Nikto"). They were pursued by the Empire, and Frax, who was worried about being put in an Imperial prison, pulled a blaster on Han. Chewbacca did a barrel roll with the *Millennium Falcon*, knocking Frax off the ship into the [Cordaxian Sea](/wiki/Cordaxian_Sea "Cordaxian Sea"). Han and Chewbacca escaped the Empire and Odona, but they left Frax behind.[[40]](#cite_note-Annual_3-40)

##### Stenness[]

:   "*It was one of my stupid schemes. To get back at a crime lord who'd been double-crossing spice smugglers.*"
:   ―Han Solo[[41]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_11-41)

Eventually, Solo would make his way to [Stenness](/wiki/Stenness "Stenness"), where he devised a plot to get revenge on a [crime lord](/wiki/Unidentified_crime_lord_(Stenness) "Unidentified crime lord (Stenness)") who operated a [gambling den](/wiki/Unidentified_gambling_den "Unidentified gambling den")[[41]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_11-41) and had continuously double-crossed spice smugglers. In order for the escapade to look as legitimate as possible, Solo and his fellow scoundrels arranged a fraudulent [marriage](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage") ceremony where Solo and the woman [Sana Starros](/wiki/Sana_Starros "Sana Starros") were illegitimately married. The robbery occurred, too, and Solo was given his share. However, Solo also took Starros' share and fled, leaving Starros in a dire situation.[[42]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_12-42) As a result, Starros came to believe that the only thing Solo was good for was lying, likening him to a "scoundrel."[[43]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_6-43)

##### Monsua Nebula[]

:   "*The Monsua Nebula. I knew it. A dog always returns to its favorite den, doesn't it?*"
:   ―Sana Starros on Han Solo returning to the Monsua Nebula[[44]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_5-44)

Solo and Chewbacca crash-landed on an [unnamed planet](/wiki/Unidentified_planet "Unidentified planet") in the [Monsua Nebula](/wiki/Monsua_Nebula "Monsua Nebula") that was entirely covered in electrical super-storms and cyclones.[[44]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_5-44) But beneath the storms lay a beautiful oasis. Solo and his copilot located a [cave](/wiki/Cave "Cave") that they turned into a secret [hiding place](/wiki/Han_Solo%27s_hiding_place "Han Solo's hiding place"), storing [Corellian wine](/wiki/Corellian_wine "Corellian wine") and other things within. He and Chewbacca used the den several times over the years.[[43]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_6-43)

### Working for Jabba the Hutt[]

Eventually, the pair came into the employment of the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord") [Jabba](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure") the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt"), who was based on the [desert](/wiki/Desert "Desert") planet [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine")[[45]](#cite_note-Episode_I-45) and was the leader of the powerful [Hutt Clan](/wiki/Hutt_Clan "Hutt Clan").[[46]](#cite_note-Eminence-46) Solo and Chewbacca smuggled for Jabba for many years,[[14]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_1-14) and Solo became Jabba's top smuggler. The smuggling duo also spent much time in [Chalmun's Spaceport Cantina](/wiki/Chalmun%27s_Spaceport_Cantina "Chalmun's Spaceport Cantina") looking for work.[[33]](#cite_note-Ultimate-33)

#### Bounty hunted[]

##### Dropping Jabba's cargo[]

:   "*You know Jabba's gonna be furious, don't you?*"  
    "*We'll have to pay him double to make up for this."*"  
    "*Or we'll be on the run, hunted by Jabba's goons wherever we go.*"
:   ―Han Solo to Chewbacca[[47]](#cite_note-CYD-47)

 [![Han and Chewie approach an Imperial blockade but escape to the planet below them.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/SoloChewbaccaBlockade-AHanAndChewieAdventure.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211221055121) [![Han and Chewie approach an Imperial blockade but escape to the planet below them.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/SoloChewbaccaBlockade-AHanAndChewieAdventure.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/265?cb=20211221055121)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/SoloChewbaccaBlockade-AHanAndChewieAdventure.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211221055121) 

Han and Chewie approach an Imperial blockade but escape to the planet below them.

 

Solo and Chewbacca were smuggling for Jabba when they were faced with an Imperial blockade. Faced with the choice of either surrendering to the Empire or dropping Jabba's cargo, they dropped the cargo, and escaped to the [planet](/wiki/Unidentified_planet_(Han_Solo) "Unidentified planet (Han Solo)") below.[[47]](#cite_note-CYD-47)

Solo and Chewbacca began repairing the *Falcon*, which was damaged in the escape, until they realized that the planet was inhabited by the crime lord [Rekias Nodo](/wiki/Rekias_Nodo "Rekias Nodo"). Posing as Jabba, he convinced Nodo to repair the ship, but he then found out that Nodo had dozens of prisoners, including [Meecha Odon](/wiki/Meecha_Odon "Meecha Odon"). Before he could act, the crime boss [Lallani](/wiki/Lallani "Lallani") showed up looking for Jabba.[[47]](#cite_note-CYD-47)

The two crime bosses started a shootout, so Solo and Chewbacca used the chaos to escape, freeing the prisoners and stealing several barrels of rhydonium in the process. Solo intended to keep the rhydonium to pay for the cargo he dropped, but Chewbacca convinced him to give it to Meecha Odon and the other freed prisoners.[[47]](#cite_note-CYD-47)

##### Nodo's revenge[]

:   "*You're Zuckuss? As in the bounty hunter?*"  
    "*Listen buddy-I don't know who's paying you, but I'll double your fee if you let me go. Triple it. What d'ya say?*"
:   ―Han Solo to Zuckess[[48]](#cite_note-FCBD_2018-48)

 [![Solo loads supplies on the Millennium Falcon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/HanLoadsSupplies-SWAFCBD2018.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181014165807) [![Solo loads supplies on the Millennium Falcon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/HanLoadsSupplies-SWAFCBD2018.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20181014165807)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/HanLoadsSupplies-SWAFCBD2018.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181014165807) 

Solo loads supplies on the *Millennium Falcon*.

 

While they were at the [space port](/wiki/Valtos_space_port "Valtos space port") on [Valtos](/wiki/Valtos "Valtos") in [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"),[[49]](#cite_note-SWHC78-49) Solo was loading supplies onto the *Millennium Falcon* when he was captured by the bounty hunters [4-LOM](/wiki/4-LOM "4-LOM") and [Zuckuss](/wiki/Zuckuss "Zuckuss"). The duo informed Solo that Nodo had put a bounty on his head. Solo, however, was hired by [Beris Ford](/wiki/Beris_Ford "Beris Ford")'s family to rescue him from the bounty hunters. Solo and Ford were freed by Chewbacca. After dumping Ford in a barrel with a homing beacon,[[48]](#cite_note-FCBD_2018-48) Solo and Chewbacca were pursued by the *[Mist Hunter](/wiki/Mist_Hunter "Mist Hunter")*. Solo and Chewbacca were forced to crash the *Falcon* on a [planet](/wiki/Unidentified_planet_(droid_uprising) "Unidentified planet (droid uprising)") in its ocean; the two bounty hunters followed them.[[50]](#cite_note-Powered_Down_1-50)

 [![Han, Chewie, 4-LOM, and Zuckuss escape a horde of droids.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/Escaping_jungle_planet_-_Adventures_11.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181013204021) [![Han, Chewie, 4-LOM, and Zuckuss escape a horde of droids.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/Escaping_jungle_planet_-_Adventures_11.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20181013204021)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/Escaping_jungle_planet_-_Adventures_11.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181013204021) 

Han, Chewie, 4-LOM, and Zuckuss escape a horde of droids.

 

The four scoundrels soon found that the planet was inhabited by a horde of droids that wanted to eradicate all life in the galaxy. The four escaped in the *Falcon*, but Han and Chewie tricked the bounty hunters into thinking that the *Falcon* lost power, and the two hunters fell for the trick, jumping back to the planet below. Han and Chewie then escaped the planet, leaving 4-LOM and Zuckuss behind.[[51]](#cite_note-Powered_Down_2-51)

#### Captured by Alinka Aloo[]

While on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") after a smuggling job, Chewbacca and Solo were approached by [Alinka Aloo](/wiki/Alinka_Aloo "Alinka Aloo"), the daughter of [Sim Aloo](/wiki/Sim_Aloo "Sim Aloo"). Aloo wanted to hire them for a job, and requested that they go to her tower. A week later, they visited Aloo, and she told them that she had a [tooka](/wiki/Tooka "Tooka")-sitting job for Chewbacca on the planet [Ushruu](/wiki/Ushruu "Ushruu"), though Solo was to remain with her. They reluctantly accepted, and Solo remained with Aloo. But she took Solo prisoner and told Chewbacca that he wouldn't be set free unless the job, which wasn't actually a tooka-sitting job, was completed. Chewbacca later returned from the failed job and broke Solo out of captivity with the help of [Mayvlin Trillick](/wiki/Mayvlin_Trillick "Mayvlin Trillick") and a bunch of [Corellian hounds](/wiki/Corellian_hound "Corellian hound"). They then escaped Coruscant and a squadron of TIE fighters, subsequently promising to fly Trillick back to her homeworld of Oktaro for free.[[52]](#cite_note-Mighty_Chewbacca-52)

#### Mission to Rendel[]

:   "*Rendel? No problem at all...for Han Solo!*"
:   ―Han Solo[[53]](#cite_note-Castle_3-53)

 [![Han is sprayed by a pink flower during the mission.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/HanSprayed-TalesFromVadersCastle3.png/revision/latest?cb=20190112232710) [![Han is sprayed by a pink flower during the mission.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/HanSprayed-TalesFromVadersCastle3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190112232710)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/HanSprayed-TalesFromVadersCastle3.png/revision/latest?cb=20190112232710) 

Han is sprayed by a pink flower during the mission.

 

After the mission to Ushruu, Han Solo and Chewbacca took a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Rendel "Mission to Rendel") to free planet [Rendel](/wiki/Rendel "Rendel") from a curse. The job was to deliver a single statuette for a one million [credits](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard"). Chewbacca was unhappy with the mission because he thought the planet was cursed. When they arrived on Rendel, they found the planet was smothered in [thorns](/wiki/Thorn "Thorn") the size of [Rancor](/wiki/Rancor "Rancor") [teeth](/wiki/Tooth "Tooth"). Right when they walked out of the *Millennium Falcon*, the tracker said that they had to deliver the statuette in the middle of a giant thorn patch. During the delivery of the statuette in the thorn patch, Solo and Chewbacca ran into a [Cranan star-hopper](/wiki/Cranan_star-hopper "Cranan star-hopper"). They found out that it was [Karamu](/wiki/Karamu "Karamu")'s and [SV-3](/wiki/SV-3 "SV-3")'s [ship](/wiki/Starship "Starship") after they found Karamu's droid Ess-Vee-Three. All of a sudden, Ess-Vee-Three said that the [Bellan](/wiki/Bellan "Bellan") the Emerald [Witch](/wiki/Witch "Witch") was waiting for him in the [forest](/wiki/Forest "Forest"). Immediately Han told Chewie that there was no witch, [vines](/wiki/Vine "Vine") must've gotten into his central processor, and there was nothing to be afraid of. Later, Han went alone to deliver the statuette because Chewie was too frightened. It wasn't long before Solo realized he should have stayed with Chewie when a vine caught his [leg](/wiki/Limb "Limb"). Solo was on the ground trying to get unstuck until he found Karamu stuck into vines. Solo tried to free him, but a [pink](/wiki/Color "Color") [flower](/wiki/Flower "Flower") sprayed Solo and made him look older. Solo was able to free Karamu, but they both got stuck later.[[53]](#cite_note-Castle_3-53)

 [![Han and Karamu are snared by Zalla's briars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/KaramuHanSnared-TalesFromVadersCastle3.png/revision/latest?cb=20190112233427) [![Han and Karamu are snared by Zalla's briars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/KaramuHanSnared-TalesFromVadersCastle3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190112233427)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/KaramuHanSnared-TalesFromVadersCastle3.png/revision/latest?cb=20190112233427) 

Han and Karamu are snared by Zalla's briars.

 

[Zalla](/wiki/Zalla "Zalla"), the sister of Bellan, the [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") of Rendel, came to Solo and Karamu and had a conversation with them about that when she cursed Rendel because she was jealous when her sister became Queen so she drove her sister off the planet, and her sister Bellan became known as the Emerald Witch. Soon after, Chewie came and saved Solo and Karamu. Solo then kicked the statuette at the Collector, and the [plants](/wiki/Plant "Plant") and vines started to die. Zalla then fell to her knees and started to sadden and die. After Zalla's death, the planet was lifted from the curse, and Chewie, Solo, and Karamu escaped on the *Millennium Falcon*.[[53]](#cite_note-Castle_3-53)

#### Treasure of Rane Mahal[]

:   "*Captain Gwarm is searching for the treasure of Rane Mahal.*"  
    "*The pirate queen? I thought she was just a legend...*"
:   ―Makkeer and Han Solo[[54]](#cite_note-Droid_Hunters-54)

At some point, during a smuggling job for Jabba the Hutt, Solo and Chewbacca stopped at [The Labyrinth](/wiki/The_Labyrinth "The Labyrinth") on [Kelada](/wiki/Kelada "Kelada"). There they ran into an [Azumel](/wiki/Azumel "Azumel") named [Makkeer](/wiki/Makkeer "Makkeer"), who was being chased by [Gwarm](/wiki/Gwarm "Gwarm"). Eventually Solo fought for Makkeer by punching Gwarm in the face. Soon after, [Lorana](/wiki/Lorana "Lorana") shot her blaster to warn Gwarm and his [gang](/wiki/Gwarm%27s_gang "Gwarm's gang") to leave. Solo asked Makkeer why Gwarm was after him. Makkeer said that Gwarm was searching for the lost treasure of [Rane Mahal](/wiki/Rane_Mahal "Rane Mahal"). Makkeer revealed that Mahal hid coordinates to the treasure in one of three [jewel](/wiki/Jewel "Jewel")-encrusted droids. Two of the droids were booby trapped. The first droid was located in [Starfarer Restaurant](/wiki/Starfarer_Restaurant "Starfarer Restaurant") on Kelada working as a [waiter](/wiki/Waiter "Waiter"). Solo, Chewie, and Makkeer went to the restaurant. Solo and Chewie drew the droid into a room. Solo called for Makkeer, but Makkeer was captured by Gwarm and his gang. When Makkeer got free, he spoke the password to the droid, which caused it to become a booby trap.[[54]](#cite_note-Droid_Hunters-54)

Solo, Chewie, and Makkeer then went to [Nubia](/wiki/Nubia "Nubia"), where the second droid was located. While on Nubia, they ran into [R5-P8](/wiki/R5-P8 "R5-P8"), a member of Gwarm's gang. They chased R5-P8 back to the gang's location and discovered that second droid was in the gang's possession. The droid ended up being a booby trap and exploded.[[54]](#cite_note-Droid_Hunters-54)

Solo, Chewie, and Makkeer then went to the planet [Ogem](/wiki/Ogem "Ogem") to find the final droid. The droid was in the hands of [Gwellis Bagnoro](/wiki/Gwellis_Bagnoro "Gwellis Bagnoro"). When they all arrived at Bagnoro's homestead, Gwarm was already there. Bagnoro's [Barghest](/wiki/Barghest "Barghest") pet [Izby](/wiki/Izby "Izby") attacked Gwarm, which allowed Solo, Chewie, and Makkeer to escape with the droid. The droid revealed the map to the lost treasure of Rane Mahal, which was located on [Sakreen](/wiki/Sakreen "Sakreen"). As they headed to Sakreen, they were followed by Gwarm and his crew. Once they arrived at Sakreen, Solo spotted Rane Mahal's galleon, but Makkeer betrayed him and Chewie and broke the *Millennium Falcon*. Makkeer also revealed that he had been working for Gwarm the entire time. The *Millennium Falcon* then crashed onto the surface. Gwarm and his crew then entered the galleon and found where the treasure was located. Solo and Chewie shot at them, and Chewie threw Makkeer at Gwarm and his gang. Solo then opened the chest and out came Rane Mahal. She revealed that there was no treasure and that she had been waiting for a ship to come so she could leave Sakreen. Solo suggested to Mahal that she take Gwarm's saucer. Mahal told her crew to load Solo, Chewie, Makkeer, Gwarm, and his gang aboard Gwarm's saucer and sell them to the first slave trader they came across. Solo and Chewie escaped. Mahal and her crew left Sakreen with Makkeer, Gwarm, and his gang. Mahal also took the droid that contained the location of Rane Mahal's fake treasure. She found out that Solo had put an ion scrambler on the droid, which caused the saucer to overload. The saucer was left in space. Solo and Chewie then blasted off aboard the *Millennium Falcon*.[[54]](#cite_note-Droid_Hunters-54)

#### Raiders of the lost urn[]

##### The father con[]

:   "*What was the ol' shipbuilder's name?*"  
    "*People call him Ovan.*"  
    "*No. It can't be…*"  
    "*What?*"  
    "*Han…that's* my *name. By the stars, I don't believe it…I've* found *you, boy.*"
:   ―Corbus Tyra, claiming to be Solo's father Ovan, and Han Solo[[8]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_1-8)

Sometime later, Solo and Chewbacca aided [Khel Tanna](/wiki/Khel_Tanna "Khel Tanna") and her [crew](/wiki/Khel_Tanna%27s_crew "Khel Tanna's crew") with a [heist](/wiki/Heist_on_Galator_III "Heist on Galator III") on [Galator III](/wiki/Galator_III "Galator III"). Though they were late to the rendezvous point, they rescued the crew from local security, with Solo ramming the *Falcon* through a [casino cruiser](/wiki/Casino_cruiser "Casino cruiser") in order to escape. Upon returning to Jabba's Palace, Solo and Chewbacca were paid for their work by Jabba. Jabba then gave them their next assignment; [stealing](/wiki/Heist_on_Corellia "Heist on Corellia") a verillix [urn](/wiki/Unidentified_urn "Unidentified urn") which contained the ashes of one of Jabba's most hated rivals, [Krestrel D'Naran](/wiki/Krestrel_D%27Naran "Krestrel D'Naran"). Offering one million credits as a reward, Jabba paired Solo and Chewbacca with the [Rodian](/wiki/Rodian "Rodian") bounty hunter [Greedo](/wiki/Greedo "Greedo") before sending the three of them to Solo's home planet of Corellia. After landing on the planet, Solo briefly talked about his upbringing with Greedo as he led them to Corellia's [Pearl District](/wiki/Pearl_District "Pearl District"). While on a rooftop, Greedo explained that they were stealing the urn from [Augustus Graves](/wiki/Augustus_Graves "Augustus Graves"), [Chief Executive Officer](/wiki/Chief_Executive_Officer "Chief Executive Officer") of the Corellian Engineering Corporation, who had the urn stored in a safe within his [penthouse](/wiki/Augustus_Graves%27_penthouse "Augustus Graves' penthouse").[[8]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_1-8)

 [![Corbus Tyra, disguised as Ovan](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/CorbusTyraOvan-HanSoloChewbacca1.png/revision/latest?cb=20220411032348) [![Corbus Tyra, disguised as Ovan](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/CorbusTyraOvan-HanSoloChewbacca1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220411032348)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2f/CorbusTyraOvan-HanSoloChewbacca1.png/revision/latest?cb=20220411032348) 

Corbus Tyra, disguised as Ovan

 

Stealing a passcard from someone exiting the building, Solo bluffed his way past security and quickly found the safe. Determining it to be a [Locris 1-42-08](/wiki/Locris_1-42-08 "Locris 1-42-08"), Solo left the building and met back up with Chewbacca and Greedo in a local bar, telling them they would need something powerful to get into the safe. Solo told them he would figure it out and his partners left the bar while he got a drink of [Montalsian ale](/wiki/Montalsian_ale "Montalsian ale"). But before he could drink it, he was bumped into by an older man, who he noticed was a worker for the Corellian Engineering Corporation. Solo offered to buy him a drink and pointed out that his father worked for the same corporation as him. When the man asked what his father's name was, Solo said it was Ovan. The man then exclaimed that Ovan was his name and claimed that he had found his son.[[8]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_1-8) In reality, the man was the criminal [Corbus Tyra](/wiki/Corbus_Tyra "Corbus Tyra").[[55]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_5-55) As Solo's supposed father tried to embrace his supposed son, Solo punched him, believing the man to be conning him. When Han accused him of faking his injury, "Ovan" removed his eye patch and revealed his scar, remarking that shipbuilding was dangerous work. To this, Solo asked "Ovan" if he had any powerful tools like a [plasma cutter](/wiki/Plasma_cutter "Plasma cutter"), which the man confirmed that he did.[[22]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_2-22)

Afterwards, Solo met back up with Chewbacca on the *Falcon*, where they discussed whether the man was actually Solo's father. When Greedo accused Solo of being sentimental, Solo explained that the man claiming to be his father was going to help them retrieve the urn. Chewbacca then pointed out that Graves had hired private security since Solo broke into his penthouse, to which Solo claimed the guards would be their way in. Later, Solo found "Ovan" at one of the docks and took the plasma cutter from him. When "Ovan" suggested going along with them for the heist, Solo refused until "Ovan" recalled a conversation he'd had with Solo on the same dock when Solo was a child. Despite Greedo's objections and Chewbacca's suspicions, Solo took his supposed father with them as they burst into a local [laundromat](/wiki/Laundromat "Laundromat") and took three guards' [security](/wiki/Locris_Syndicated_Securities "Locris Syndicated Securities") uniforms. While Chewbacca retrieved their getaway speeder, "Ovan" bluffed his way past security, who allowed him, Solo and Greedo to enter the premises in their disguises. After talking with "Ovan" about surviving on Corellia while using the turbolift, Solo had Greedo break the electrolock sealing the entrance to the penthouse. When Greedo was unable to break the lock, Solo told "Ovan" to open the turbolift doors in case they needed to escape. Solo then called one of the actual guards and asked them to remotely deactivate the lock due to it malfunctioning.[[22]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_2-22)

The guard did so, letting the three into the penthouse. Once they were inside, Solo told Greedo to stand watch and not touch anything while he and "Ovan" worked on opening the safe. While they did so, Solo asked his apparent father why he hadn't asked about his cut of the reward. When the man claiming to be his father asked Solo to trust him, Solo reminded "Ovan" of his upbringing and lack of trust in others. "Ovan" then gave Solo a recording that seemed to be of them together during Solo's childhood. When Solo claimed he didn't do sentiment, "Ovan" said he just wanted to get to know his supposed son better. Solo thanked "Ovan" for the recording and revealed that he still had the dice from when he was a child, though requested that he not to tell anyone. As they started working on the safe, Solo contacted Chewbacca to check on his progress. However, he ended the call once they opened the safe and saw that it was empty. Solo confronted Greedo over his bad intel and quickly realized that he had taken an expensive item he wasn't supposed to. Tagged with an MSX tracker, the item set off an alarm and alerted security of the break-in. Solo ran for the turbolift and opened the door to escape, only to be met by a group of armed security guards.[[22]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_2-22)

Greedo pulled out his blaster and tried firing at the guards, though the blast only bounced off of the transparisteel windows. From Greedo's failed plan, Solo got an idea and called another group of guards for medical assistance, hoping they were unaware of what had happened. From there, he called Chewbacca and told him to forget about the speeder and come to their location. Solo then retrieved the plasma cutter and used it to break one of the windows. Minutes later, more guards arrived with a medshuttle and Solo stunned the driver before he, "Ovan" and Greedo used it to escape from the penthouse. They then met back up with Chewbacca and used a landspeeder to reach the *Falcon*. Once they arrived, Solo told his supposed father that Graves' terminal said the urn had been sold to a buyer on [Antillion](/wiki/Antillion "Antillion") and that he and Chewbacca could use an extra pair of hands. "Ovan" accepted the offer and joined them aboard the *Falcon*. When "Ovan" asked Solo if they would wait for Greedo to join them before they left Corellia, Solo said he only went along with Greedo because he claimed to know the location of the urn, which he clearly hadn't. Solo went on to say that the reward would only be split three ways as they left Greedo on Corellia and headed for Antillion.[[56]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_3-56)

##### Losing the *Falcon*[]

:   "*What's he saying?*"  
    "*That I got played. That my "dad" faked being unconscious and took the urn with him when Chewie took him on board the* Falcon*…and then he* took *the* Falcon*. I'm gonna* kill *that guy. As many times as I have to.*"
:   ―Khel Tanna and Han Solo[[55]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_5-55)

Once they arrived on Antillion, Solo went on to explain that the urn had been sold to a [Sava](/wiki/Sava "Sava") named [Madelin Sun](/wiki/The_Archivist "The Archivist"). When his supposed father doubted anyone on such a planet could buy the urn, Solo speculated that she may have traded something for it. Upon locating Sun's shop, Solo said he would negotiate for the urn. However, when Sun denied having any such urn in her possession, Solo told "Ovan" and Chewbacca that she definitely had it and that they would have to get her away from her collection. When "Ovan" asked him if he had a plan, Solo said he would inform the local stormtroopers of illegal contraband in her possession. After he did so, Solo, "Ovan" and Chewbacca watched from a distance as the stormtroopers raided Sun's shop. Sun was then assisted by a mysterious person with whom she left in a ship. Solo told Chewbacca to wait for him and "Ovan" in the *Falcon* while they retrieved the urn from the shop. Upon entering the shop, they found that the stormtroopers had been killed. "Ovan" then found the urn amidst a pile of artifacts. But before they could leave, Solo's supposed father was suddenly stunned before Solo found himself in the grip of the Wookiee bounty hunter [Krrsantan](/wiki/Krrsantan "Krrsantan").[[56]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_3-56)

Solo fought Krrsantan briefly, but was knocked out and taken to [Mollo Tanka](/wiki/Mollo_Tanka "Mollo Tanka"). Once he awoke, he found himself in the presence of Augustus Graves, who demanded to know the urn's location. After an unsuccessful interrogation, Solo was found by Chewbacca, who proceeded to fight off Krrsantan in a death duel. Subduing the [mercenary](/wiki/Mercenary "Mercenary") with a thermal detonator, Chewbacca fled with Solo from Graves' palace, only to find that the *Falcon* was gone.[[57]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_4-57) They were then surrounded by Krrsantan and Graves' guards, but were quickly rescued by Tanna's crew and brought aboard their [ship](/wiki/Enigma_Catalyst "Enigma Catalyst"). Once they were safe, Tanna punched Solo as payback for stranding them earlier. With [T'onga](/wiki/T%27onga "T'onga"), [Akko](/wiki/Akko "Akko") and [Ooris Bynar](/wiki/Ooris_Bynar "Ooris Bynar") beside Tanna, Solo admitted he was grateful before he was punched by Greedo for leaving him on Corellia. When Tanna asked Solo where the urn was, he said it was back on Antillion, but that they first had to find the *Falcon* and his father. Tanna's crew aimed their blasters at Solo and insisted on retrieving the urn first, to which Solo agreed.[[55]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_5-55)

Solo and Chewbacca led the crew back to the shop on Antillion, only to find that the urn was gone. Chewbacca then realized that "Ovan" was an imposter and that he had faked being unconscious so he could make off with the urn and the *Falcon*. Revealing there were moments where he had not believed the conman, Solo used a tracker he had planted on his fake father as insurance to locate him. Solo, Chewbacca, Greedo and Tanna's crew followed the tracker to where the conman had been detained: the [Benelex Marshal Service](/wiki/Benelex_Marshal_Service "Benelex Marshal Service") [Headquarters](/wiki/Benelex_Marshal_Service_Headquarters "Benelex Marshal Service Headquarters") on [Paqualis III](/wiki/Paqualis_III "Paqualis III"). Tanna had Solo take control of the ship along with T'onga and Akko while the rest of them went for the conman, warning him not to damage her ship. Solo provided cover fire as Chewbacca, Greedo, Tanna and Bynar retrieved the conman, whom they learned was named Corbus Tyra. However, as they brought him aboard the ship, Chewbacca was blasted and placed under arrest by [Marshal](/wiki/Marshal "Marshal") [Buck Vancto](/wiki/Buck_Vancto "Buck Vancto"). Solo tried to stop the crew from leaving without Chewbacca, but he was shot in the chest by Greedo.[[55]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_5-55)

Rather than helping Solo, Tanna's crew dropped him off on [Escalan](/wiki/Escalan "Escalan"). After washing up on shore, Solo was found by [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Aber](/wiki/Aber "Aber"), who heard him mutter his own name as she brought him to a spare bed.[[58]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_6-58) After healing, Solo went to a local bar, but was kicked out due to not speaking the native language. He then saw a broadcast reporting on the impending executions of three prisoners in a Benelex Marshal Service [prison](/wiki/Gulhadar_prison "Gulhadar prison") on [Gulhadar](/wiki/Gulhadar_III "Gulhadar III"). After seeing that Chewbacca was among the prisoners, Solo found a local who spoke [Basic](/wiki/Galactic_Basic_Standard "Galactic Basic Standard") and got them to fly him to Gulhadar. Upon reaching the prison, they picked up Chewbacca, [Phaedra](/wiki/Phaedra "Phaedra") and the pirate [Maz Kanata](/wiki/Maz_Kanata "Maz Kanata"), who were in the midst of escaping. After dropping off Kanata at her [castle](/wiki/Takodana_Castle "Takodana Castle") on [Takodana](/wiki/Takodana "Takodana"), Solo and Chewbacca flew to Tatooine along with Phaedra. Once they entered Chalmun's Cantina, they found Greedo and interrogated him for the *Falcon*'s location.[[59]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_7-59) After being thrown out onto the street by Chewbacca, Greedo confessed that the *Falcon* was in a docking bay in [Mos Entha](/wiki/Mos_Entha "Mos Entha"). Before he had split from Tanna's crew, Greedo had cheated in a game of Sabacc to gain ownership of the *Falcon*. Greedo also admitted that the urn had been confiscated by [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") and stored within his [office](/wiki/Grand_Moff_Tarkin%27s_office "Grand Moff Tarkin's office") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"). After punching Greedo and leaving him unconscious in the street, Solo reclaimed the *Falcon* and discussed the situation with Chewbacca and Phaedra. Solo claimed the heist would be impossible, due to the office being guarded by [death troopers](/wiki/Death_trooper "Death trooper"). However, Phaedra explained that she had a plan.[[60]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_8-60)

##### Core issues[]

:   "*Ajax was different. He was perhaps the only droid who can truly be said to be 'free'. And he was* determined *to bring that freedom to droids across the galaxy.*"  
    "*Yeah. I knew a droid like that once. Didn't work out too well for her.*"
:   ―Korin Pers and Han Solo, on Ajax Sigma and L3-37, respectively[[61]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_9-61)

 [![Han Solo tries to save Chewbacca from a dangerous fall.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/HanTriesToSaveChewie-HanSoloChewbacca8.png/revision/latest?cb=20230924012726) [![Han Solo tries to save Chewbacca from a dangerous fall.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/HanTriesToSaveChewie-HanSoloChewbacca8.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230924012726)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/HanTriesToSaveChewie-HanSoloChewbacca8.png/revision/latest?cb=20230924012726) 

Han Solo tries to save Chewbacca from a dangerous fall.

 

Upon arriving on Coruscant, Solo and Chewbacca posed as sanitation workers and snuck through the planet's sewer system while Phaedra posed as a protocol droid. Once she convinced Tarkin to leave his office, Solo and Chewbacca blew their way inside, allowing Solo to retrieve the urn. Surrounded by stormtroopers, Phaedra broke a nearby window and the three of them jumped out before landing on a passing train. But before they could escape, they were caught by a stormtrooper, who blasted Chewbacca and sent him falling over the side of the train.[[60]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_8-60) As he fell though, Chewbacca managed to grab onto a passing vehicle and throw off the Imperial driver, allowing him to fly to safety. Just then, the train made a sharp turn, cuasing Solo to lose grip of the urn. Luckily, Phaedra was able to catch it as they leapt off the train onto a nearby platform. She then opened the urn and was surprised to instead find a [neural core](/wiki/Neural_core "Neural core") inside.[[61]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_9-61)

Regrouping on the *Falcon*, the group realized that Jabba had lied about the urn's contents. As Phaedra doubted that they should even bring Jabba the core, Solo said they would first find out the core's origins from an Ugnaught sava named [Korin Pers](/wiki/Korin_Pers "Korin Pers"), who had connections with Calrissian. Traveling to the "Smuggler's Moon" of [Nar Shaddaa](/wiki/Nar_Shaddaa "Nar Shaddaa"), the group found Pers in her [office](/wiki/Korin_Pers%27_office "Korin Pers' office"). Pretending to hate Calrissian to gain favor, Solo asked Pers if she knew anything about the core. After studying it, Pers explained that it was the core of an ancient droid named [Ajax Sigma](/wiki/Ajax_Sigma "Ajax Sigma"). A droid revolutionary, Sigma had led an uprising of droids over two centuries ago. Sigma eventually led a droid [uprising](/wiki/Kligson%27s_Moon_Uprising "Kligson's Moon Uprising") on [Kligson's Moon](/wiki/Kligson%27s_Moon "Kligson's Moon") to bring about the [emancipation](/wiki/Manumission "Manumission") of all synthetic life. After killing many organics during battle, Sigma was finally destroyed by the Jedi of the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"). Reminded of L3-37, Solo asked Pers what someone would want with a droid like Sigma. When Pers said Sigma would be a formidable assassin, Phaedra insisted they not give Sigma's core to Jabba.[[61]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_9-61)

 [![Han Solo and Chewbacca with the neural core of Ajax Sigma.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Revelations1-SoloandChewie.png/revision/latest?cb=20230924013010) [![Han Solo and Chewbacca with the neural core of Ajax Sigma.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Revelations1-SoloandChewie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230924013010)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Revelations1-SoloandChewie.png/revision/latest?cb=20230924013010) 

Han Solo and Chewbacca with the neural core of Ajax Sigma.

 

However, they were interrupted by the arrival of Tanna's crew. As they opened fire inside the office, Solo took the core and ran for the exit along with Chewbacca and Phaedra, only to be stopped by Vancto. Chewbacca fought Vancto while Solo and Phaedra returned to the *Falcon* with the core. But they were then confronted by Tyra, who held them at blaster point and demanded they hand over the core.[[61]](#cite_note-Han_Chewie_9-61) In the end, Solo and Chewbacca would decide to bury the core.[[62]](#cite_note-Revelations_1-62)

### Galactic Civil War[]

#### A fateful business venture[]

:   "*Seventeen-thousand! Those guys must really be desperate—this could really save my neck. Get back to the ship and get her ready.*"
:   ―Han Solo, to Chewbacca, after meeting with Kenobi and Skywalker[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

 [![Solo and Chewbacca negotiate passage fees with Kenobi and Skywalker in Chalmun's Cantina.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/Charter_negotiations.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150715001118) [![Solo and Chewbacca negotiate passage fees with Kenobi and Skywalker in Chalmun's Cantina.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/Charter_negotiations.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150715001118)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/Charter_negotiations.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150715001118) 

Solo and Chewbacca negotiate passage fees with Kenobi and Skywalker in Chalmun's Cantina.

 

After dropping a cargo of [Kessel spice](/wiki/Glitterstim "Glitterstim")[[33]](#cite_note-Ultimate-33) they were smuggling for Jabba, Solo and Chewbacca had a 50,000-credit bounty placed on their heads. In trying to pay off Jabba, they traveled to Chalmun's Cantina on Tatooine, where they looked for work.[[63]](#cite_note-Character_Encyclopedia-63) While Chewbacca left the table, Solo took the opportunity to flirt with a B-girl[[64]](#cite_note-SW:CL-64) named [Jenny](/wiki/Jenny "Jenny"). She sat on Solo's lap and the two witnessed[[65]](#cite_note-ANH:TP,tS,atFB-65) a bar brawl between the [exiled](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)") [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") and the criminals [Ponda Baba](/wiki/Ponda_Baba "Ponda Baba") and [Cornelius Evazan](/wiki/Cornelius_Evazan "Cornelius Evazan"), who had physically assaulted [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), leading Kenobi to cut off Baba's arm with [his](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi%27s_third_lightsaber "Obi-Wan Kenobi's third lightsaber") [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber").[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6) As Chewbacca joined them, Jenny realized that Solo didn't even remember her name, leading her to throw the remainder of Solo's drink in his face before storming off.[[65]](#cite_note-ANH:TP,tS,atFB-65)

Afterwards, Kenobi and Skywalker made their way to Solo's booth, Kenobi having talked with Chewie before the brawl. They arrived and began negotiating. Solo assured Kenobi that the *Millennium Falcon* was the fastest ship around, because it had made the Kessel Run in less than twelve parsecs. Kenobi informed Solo that the cargo was only himself, Skywalker, two droids, and no questions asked beyond an admission that they wanted to avoid Imperials entirely. Therefore, Solo set the price at 10,000 credits—higher than he normally would have. However, Kenobi raised Solo's bid to 17,000 credits: 2,000 in advance and 15,000 when they reached Alderaan. His interest piqued at such a sum offered when it was so needed, Solo quickly accepted the deal. The smuggler then told his temporary employer to meet him in [Docking Bay 94](/wiki/Docking_Bay_94 "Docking Bay 94") for departure as soon as he was ready, before warning Kenobi that some Imperial [sandtroopers](/wiki/Desert_stormtrooper "Desert stormtrooper") had entered the cantina and were looking for Evazan and Baba's attacker. Kenobi and Skywalker hastily fled, leaving Solo to express his elation to Chewbacca at having garnered such a high-paying job to pay off Jabba. Chewbacca left as well right after.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

 [![Solo prepares to blast Greedo from under the table.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Poe_Dameron_14_Star_Wars_40th.png/revision/latest?cb=20190119220153) [![Solo prepares to blast Greedo from under the table.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Poe_Dameron_14_Star_Wars_40th.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20190119220153)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Poe_Dameron_14_Star_Wars_40th.png/revision/latest?cb=20190119220153) 

Solo prepares to blast Greedo from under the table.

 

As Solo got up to leave, he was confronted by Greedo, who demanded to be paid Jabba's debt, or he would take Solo's dead body back to Jabba as payment. Solo, then, in self defense, covertly pulled his [DL-44](/wiki/DL-44_heavy_blaster_pistol "DL-44 heavy blaster pistol") [blaster pistol](/wiki/Blaster_pistol "Blaster pistol") under the table; after Greedo tried to shoot Solo but missed, Solo fired back, killing the Rodian.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6) Solo ignored the [Murder tax](/wiki/Murder_tax "Murder tax")[[66]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_4-66) Jabba enforced on Tatooine, opting instead to simply toss [Wuher](/wiki/Wuher "Wuher"), the cantina's [bartender](/wiki/Bartender "Bartender"), some [credit chips](/wiki/Credit_chip "Credit chip"), before apologizing for leaving a mess and then heading to Docking Bay 94.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6) None of the witnesses present could agree whether Solo or Greedo shot first, but all confirmed Solo had the better shot of the two.[[67]](#cite_note-Secrets-67)

Solo arrived in the docking and found Jabba himself, with several of his guards—including[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6) Jabba's top bounty hunter [Boba Fett](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett")—[[33]](#cite_note-Ultimate-33) looking for him near the *Falcon*. Jabba inquired whether Solo was going to pay him, and why he had "fried poor Greedo." Jabba was disappointed in having to put the bounty on Solo,[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6) the crime lord's top smuggler.[[33]](#cite_note-Ultimate-33) Solo insisted he had had no choice but to dump the cargo, and informed the Hutt that he had secured a charter that would be able to compensate the Hutt's loss in full as soon as he completed it. Jabba was pleased and added that if Solo paid twenty percent interest all could be forgotten, but Solo talked him down to fifteen percent, and ironically stated that the Hutt was a "wonderful Human being," before boarding the *Falcon*.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

A short time later, Kenobi, Skywalker, and their two droids, the [protocol droid](/wiki/Protocol_droid "Protocol droid") [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO") and the [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2"), boarded the *Falcon* after Skywalker remarked that the *Falcon* appeared to be a "piece of junk." Solo corrected him: The *Millennium Falcon* looked out of shape, but had been given "special modifications" that made it one of the fastest ships in the galaxy. Just then, a [squad](/wiki/Squadron "Squadron") of stormtroopers appeared in the docking bay and opened fire on Solo. Solo fired back while retreating on board and shouted for Chewbacca to take off. The *Falcon* blasted away from the Mos Eisley spaceport and clear of Tatooine. As the *Falcon* entered space, Solo realized that his passengers were even more wanted by the Empire than he thought as multiple Star Destroyers pursued his ship. Trying to dodge Imperial fire while addressing the boy's annoying backseat badgering about the necessity of proper navigation for travel through hyperspace, Solo inserted coordinates to the Alderaan system into the *Falcon*'s [navigation computer](/wiki/Navigation_computer "Navigation computer") and made the jump to [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace"), escaping their pursuers.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

 [![The Millennium Falcon's passengers pass the time while traveling to Alderaan.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/Falcon-lounge.png/revision/latest?cb=20130311221516) [![The Millennium Falcon's passengers pass the time while traveling to Alderaan.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/Falcon-lounge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20130311221516)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e6/Falcon-lounge.png/revision/latest?cb=20130311221516) 

The *Millennium Falcon*'s passengers pass the time while traveling to Alderaan.

 

While en route to Alderaan, Solo boasted of outrunning the "Imperial [slugs](/wiki/Slug_(creature) "Slug (creature)")," but was annoyed when no one would humor him, considering Luke was concerned with Kenobi who himself was troubled by a great disturbance in the Force resulting from what turned out to be the destruction of Alderaan. Chewbacca and R2-D2, often shortened to Artoo, were playing a game of [Dejarik](/wiki/Dejarik "Dejarik") when Artoo outplayed the Wookiee, so Solo warned the droids not to upset him because Wookiee rage was not something C-3PO, often shortened to Threepio, a droid programmed in protocol, would want to experience. Skywalker, meanwhile, trained with a [remote](/wiki/Marksman-H_training_remote "Marksman-H training remote") with [his lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber"), trying to deflect the sting bolts with the civilized weapon. Solo was skeptical of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force")—the energy field that connected all living things in the galaxy, and the Jedi, like Kenobi, were able to use to perform seemingly supernatural feats—because in all his travels he had never seen proof of its existence; to Solo, "There's no mystical energy field that controls my [destiny](/wiki/Destiny "Destiny")" and it was all "simple tricks and nonsense." Kenobi took Solo's skepticism as a challenge and put a helmet over Luke's face so he couldn't see. Skywalker tried to deflect the bolts again, and did, while unable to see. Solo was mildly impressed, but attributed Skywalker's ability to luck.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

 [![The Falcon is pulled into the Death Star by the station's tractor beams.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/Tractor_beam_falcon_death_star_recrop.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150722042829) [![The Falcon is pulled into the Death Star by the station's tractor beams.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/Tractor_beam_falcon_death_star_recrop.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150722042829)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/Tractor_beam_falcon_death_star_recrop.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150722042829) 

The *Falcon* is pulled into the Death Star by the station's tractor beams.

 

Soon, the *Falcon* emerged from hyperspace in the Alderaan system. The *Falcon* came out at Alderaan's galactic coordinates, but into a [meteor shower](/wiki/Meteor_shower "Meteor shower"), with Alderaan nowhere in sight. Kenobi, using the Force, realized the [asteroid](/wiki/Asteroid "Asteroid") field was Alderaan: The entire planet had been destroyed by the Empire. Solo couldn't believe the Empire had had enough firepower to do so, even with their entire fleet, but then an Imperial short-range TIE fighter appeared, seemingly confirming Kenobi's suspicions. Skywalker and Solo both worried that if the fighter identified them as the freighter that had blasted away from Tatooine, they would be damned. Therefore, Solo got in range to destroy it. Kenobi, however, argued against it before Solo realized that the fighter did have a base—what appeared to be a small moon in the distance. Kenobi quickly surmised that the body was not a moon, but an Imperial [space station](/wiki/Space_station "Space station"), the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station") [battle station](/wiki/Battle_station "Battle station") equipped with a [superlaser](/wiki/Superlaser "Superlaser") capable of destroying entire planets. Solo was shocked at the Death Star's 120-[kilometer](/wiki/Kilometer "Kilometer") spherical diameter and prepared to turn the *Falcon* around and retreat. One of the station's [tractor beams](/wiki/Tractor_beam "Tractor beam"), however, began to pull the *Falcon* in. Solo prepared to fight his way out once they were taken aboard and shut the freighter down. Kenobi was able to talk Solo into listening to him, though: hide instead of fight. Therefore, they ejected the *Falcon*'s five [Model CEC Class-1](/wiki/CEC_Class-1_escape_pod "CEC Class-1 escape pod") [escape pods](/wiki/Escape_pod "Escape pod") and hid themselves in the *Falcon*'s [smuggling compartments](/wiki/Smuggling_compartment "Smuggling compartment") located under the floor.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

#### Rescuing the Princess of Alderaan[]

:   "*Wonderful girl! Either I'm gonna kill her, or I'm beginning to like her!*"
:   ―Solo to Skywalker, after Organa took the lead in their escape[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

The freighter was pulled into [Docking Bay 327](/wiki/Docking_Bay_327 "Docking Bay 327") where it was boarded and quickly searched by stormtroopers on the orders of [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"),[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6) the Emperor's chief enforcer and a [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith").[[68]](#cite_note-Vader_Databank-68) After the troopers left, Solo and the others emerged from the compartments and Kenobi devised a plan to disable the tractor beam from inside the station. As they worked out the plan's details, an Imperial [scanning](/wiki/Sensor "Sensor") crew came aboard to more thoroughly search the ship. Solo shot them and then impersonated the crew, yelling out to a pair of stormtroopers outside for assistance. They came, Solo shot them, and he and Skywalker dressed themselves in [their armor](/wiki/Stormtrooper_armor "Stormtrooper armor").[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

 [![Solo and Skywalker argue over whether to rescue the princess imprisoned aboard the Death Star.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Han_luke_stormarmor.png/revision/latest?cb=20130312012317) [![Solo and Skywalker argue over whether to rescue the princess imprisoned aboard the Death Star.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Han_luke_stormarmor.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130312012317)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/Han_luke_stormarmor.png/revision/latest?cb=20130312012317) 

Solo and Skywalker argue over whether to rescue the princess imprisoned aboard the Death Star.

 

Skywalker, now under the guise trooper [TK-421](/wiki/TK-421 "TK-421"), fooled an officer into opening the door to the hangar's [control room](/wiki/Docking_Control_Room_327 "Docking Control Room 327"). Chewbacca and Solo cut down the officer and his comrades, while Artoo plugged into a computer terminal to locate the tractor beam controls. Artoo found them and Kenobi departed to disable it after commanding the others to stay in the control room. Solo was fine with staying; he'd gotten much more than the he's signed on for in the cantina. Artoo, however, had learned that [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") of Alderaan and a leading member of the Rebel Alliance, was aboard the station, and was scheduled to be executed in [Detention Block AA-23](/wiki/Detention_Block_AA-23 "Detention Block AA-23") very soon. Skywalker insisted that they go [rescue her](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia "Rescue of Princess Leia"), and reasoned that if Kenobi had known she was present, he would have gone after her, too. Solo at first refused, but decided it was worth the risk when Skywalker and Chewbacca assured him there would be a huge reward from the Rebel Alliance if she was rescued. Skywalker quickly worked out a subterfuge to bluff their way into the prison using Chewbacca as a prisoner scheduled for a prisoner transfer.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

Soon thereafter, they set out to the fifth level of the Death Star with their "prisoner" in [stuncuffs](/wiki/Stuncuffs "Stuncuffs") and left the droids behind. They arrived at the detention level and told the officer in charge, [Shann Childsen](/wiki/Shann_Childsen "Shann Childsen"), of the supposed transfer. He went to check the legitimacy of the fake stormtroopers' claim, while other troopers went to detain the Wookiee. Chewbacca, per the plan, attacked. Solo kept up the charade while firing on the guards and [security cameras](/wiki/Security_camera "Security camera"). Solo located the princess' cell in the prison computer and sent Skywalker to get her while he tried to convince an [officer](/wiki/Officer "Officer"),[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6) [Ensign](/wiki/Ensign "Ensign") [Toos](/wiki/Toos "Toos"),[[69]](#cite_note-End_of_Watch-69) that nothing had gone wrong on their level via the [comm system](/wiki/Comm_unit "Comm unit") on a ["Tulip" style Imperial work station](/wiki/%22Tulip%22_style_Imperial_work_station "\"Tulip\" style Imperial work station"). In the end, a nervous Solo gave up and shot the panel when the tech saw through the ruse and sent stormtroopers to investigate.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

 [![Organa takes command of her own rescue mission and orders Solo to jump into a garbage chute.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Into_the_garbage_chute_flyboy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150722043546) [![Organa takes command of her own rescue mission and orders Solo to jump into a garbage chute.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Into_the_garbage_chute_flyboy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150722043546)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Into_the_garbage_chute_flyboy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150722043546) 

Organa takes command of her own rescue mission and orders Solo to jump into a garbage chute.

 

After Solo warned Skywalker of the incoming soldiers, the troopers blockaded the only exit to the detention block and attacked. Solo and Chewbacca returned fire while they retreated to Skywalker's position. Skywalker had gotten the princess, who critiqued their plan to rescue her without thinking through an escape route. Solo quipped that she was welcome to return to her cell and be executed rather than rescued if she desired, while they took cover in the corridor and traded fire with the Imperials. Organa lost patience with the three men, took a blaster and shot open a chute and dove in after telling the others to follow. Solo remarked to Skywalker that he wasn't sure if he was very frustrated with Organa, or if he was beginning to like her, and shoved Chewbacca into the chute. Skywalker and Solo followed right after.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

They found themselves in a [garbage compactor](/wiki/Garbage_masher_3263827 "Garbage masher 3263827") with the only exit locked. Solo sarcastically told Organa great work in getting them nowhere and tried to shoot the open the exit. The laser bounced wildly around the [compactor](/wiki/Garbage_compactor "Garbage compactor"), nearly hitting the rebels. Skywalker informed Solo that he had already tried it, that it was [magnetically sealed](/wiki/Magnetic_seal "Magnetic seal"). Organa commanded Solo to put his blaster away. Solo was unhappy at being ordered around, but did so. Just then, a low growl sounded; the four simultaneously realized they weren't alone. A moment later, a tentacle belonging to a [dianoga](/wiki/Omi "Omi") grabbed Skywalker and pulled him under water. Solo and Organa frantically searched for him, and seconds later he reemerged. Solo grabbed Skywalker and tried to shoot the [creature](/wiki/Dianoga "Dianoga"), but Skywalker was pulled under again. Solo had almost given up looking when the dianoga released him and vanished. Solo helped him up, before the walls of the compactor began to close in. Chewbacca the princess and Solo tried to brace them while Skywalker contacted the droids in order for Artoo to hack into the station's network and shut down the compactor. After a bit of a delay, Artoo succeeded. The three Humans and the Wookiee rejoiced, for their lives had been saved.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

 [![Solo and Chewbacca flee from pursuing stormtroopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/Star_Wars_36_Star_Wars_40th.png/revision/latest?cb=20190120213733) [![Solo and Chewbacca flee from pursuing stormtroopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/Star_Wars_36_Star_Wars_40th.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20190120213733)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/Star_Wars_36_Star_Wars_40th.png/revision/latest?cb=20190120213733) 

Solo and Chewbacca flee from pursuing stormtroopers.

 

They left the compactor and Skywalker and Solo took off the trooper armor. As they did so, Chewbacca heard strange noises coming from the compactor and ran away. Solo fired a laser blast into the compactor to prove that the Wookiee was acting with cowardice. Organa scolded him for making so much noise, and told him that he would have to take orders from her if they were going to survive the ordeal. Solo was appalled at Organa's demeanor, and informed "her worshipfulness" that he only took orders from himself. Leaving Organa to quip that it was amazing that the smuggler was still alive. Solo looked at Skywalker and muttered that no reward was worth putting up with the princess' attitude.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

As the group made their way back towards the docking bay, they ran into a group of stormtroopers. Solo yelled for Skywalker and Organa to go to the *Falcon* while he and his first mate charged the troopers. The troopers turned and ran from the screaming smuggler. Solo, however, ran into the troopers' reinforcements, and then he was being chased. He ran back into the hangar and through a [blast door](/wiki/Blast_door "Blast door") as it closed, stopping the troopers who had pursued him and Chewbacca. Solo caught up with Skywalker and Organa, who had also run into some trouble, and they prepared to board the *Falcon*, but several stormtroopers stood guard outside. The troopers, however, rushed to Darth Vader, who was locked in [lightsaber combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat") with Kenobi. The group took advantage of the distraction Kenobi had created to rush aboard the freighter—except for Skywalker, who stopped. Kenobi saw that Skywalker and the others would be safe, so he let himself be cut down by the Dark Lord. Skywalker yelled in grief, alerting the troopers to their presence. The troopers opened fire, but Solo ran and started his ship, and once everyone was on board, blasted off and away from the battle station. Their troubles were not over, however: four Imperial TIE fighters were in pursuit.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

 [![Solo tells Organa that he's only in it for the money.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/InItForTheMoney-SWZ85.png/revision/latest?cb=20210228065438) [![Solo tells Organa that he's only in it for the money.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/InItForTheMoney-SWZ85.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20210228065438)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/InItForTheMoney-SWZ85.png/revision/latest?cb=20210228065438) 

Solo tells Organa that he's only in it for the money.

 

Chewbacca piloted the *Falcon* in order for Skywalker and Solo to man its turrets to fight off the attackers. A dogfight ensued, where Solo shot down one fighter and congratulated Skywalker when he shot one down, as well—and advised him to not "get cocky." Solo soon shot down the final Imperial fighter and sighed in relief as they entered hyperspace to travel to [Yavin 4](/wiki/Yavin_4 "Yavin 4")—the location of the Rebels' [hidden base](/wiki/Great_Temple "Great Temple"). While en route to the [Yavin system](/wiki/Yavin_system "Yavin system"), Organa grimly informed Solo that the Imperials had let them escape in order to track them to the hidden base, which explained the relative ease of their escape. Solo didn't believe it had been easy and demanded to know what information Artoo was carrying that made him so special. Organa told him: the [technical readouts](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans") to the Death Star. Solo was shocked, and added that once he was rewarded, he was going to leave; he claimed he wasn't interested in the Rebels' revolution or the princess as a companion. Organa assured Solo that if all he loved was money, that's all he would receive, and stomped away. Skywalker took her place and asked the smuggler what he thought of the princess. Solo admitted she had spirit, and inquired to whether Skywalker could see Organa and Solo together. Skywalker quickly said "no," thereby admitting he had his own feeling for the princess—much to Solo's amusement.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

#### A change of conscience[]

:   "*I knew you'd come back—I just knew it!*"  
    "*Well, I couldn't let you get all the credit and take all the reward!*"  
    "*Hey, I knew there was more to you than money!*"
:   ―Skywalker, Solo, and Organa celebrate the destruction of the Death Star[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

 [![Solo and his friends arrive at the Rebel base on Yavin 4.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/Yavin_4_Temple.png/revision/latest?cb=20121227220518) [![Solo and his friends arrive at the Rebel base on Yavin 4.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/Yavin_4_Temple.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/259?cb=20121227220518)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/Yavin_4_Temple.png/revision/latest?cb=20121227220518) 

Solo and his friends arrive at the Rebel base on Yavin 4.

 

The *Falcon* soon reached Yavin 4, where Solo and the others were welcomed; Alliance [Alliance High Command](/wiki/Alliance_High_Command "Alliance High Command") had feared that Organa had died with her world. The plans within Artoo were analyzed and a weakness was discovered: a two-meter wide [exhaust port](/wiki/Thermal_exhaust_port "Thermal exhaust port") that led to the station's main [reactor](/wiki/Reactor "Reactor"). Solo and Chewbacca attended a briefing for the [Rebel pilots](/wiki/Rebel_pilot "Rebel pilot"), including Skywalker, who were going to attack the station when it inevitably arrived. [General](/wiki/General "General") [Jan Dodonna](/wiki/Jan_Dodonna "Jan Dodonna") explained that a one-man starfighter could get close enough and fire [proton torpedoes](/wiki/Proton_torpedo "Proton torpedo") into the shaft that would cause a chain reaction that would destroy the station. Solo was skeptical, thinking it [suicide](/wiki/Death "Death") to even attempt. Therefore, after he was given his reward of credits, he packed up to leave, but was confronted by Skywalker who insisted he stay and fight with the Rebellion. Solo, thinking selfishly of his debt with Jabba, refused, and asked Skywalker to come with him and Chewbacca. Skywalker was dismayed with Solo's selfishness and angrily walked away. Solo called after him an old Jedi saying: "[May the Force be with you](/wiki/May_the_Force_be_with_you "May the Force be with you")." Chewbacca was disappointed in Solo—he wanted to stay and fight.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

Solo and Chewbacca then left Yavin 4 aboard the *Millennium Falcon*. Soon, however, Chewbacca's nagging and Solo's conscience got the better of the smuggler, and he turned around and headed towards the Death Star, where the [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin") was raging—although he did so not for the Rebellion's cause, but to save his friend, Skywalker.[[70]](#cite_note-Han_Insider-70) He arrived in his ship to find Skywalker in his [T-65B X-wing starfighter](/wiki/T-65B_X-wing_starfighter "T-65B X-wing starfighter") being pursued by three TIE fighters, led by Darth Vader, in the station's [meridian trench](/wiki/Meridian_trench "Meridian trench"). Solo fired on the three Imperial fighters, destroying one, and causing another to panic and collide with Vader, who was sent spinning away from the battle station. Solo yelled in glee and told Skywalker to fire his torpedoes, since he was now clear to do so. Skywalker did, and it was a direct hit: The Death Star blew apart[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6) and killed everyone on board.[[71]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_1-71) Vader, however, escaped after regaining control of his fighter. Of the thirty Alliance ships that had participated in the battle, only three returned to the base with Solo in the *Falcon*. Solo rushed to Skywalker as he exited [his fighter](/wiki/Red_Five_(T-65B_X-wing_starfighter) "Red Five (T-65B X-wing starfighter)") and congratulated him, while the princess embraced Solo for his bravery and proving there was more to him than money.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6)

 [![Organa awards Solo and Skywalker for their selflessness during the Battle of Yavin.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/Leia_honors_Han_and_Luke.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151023234158) [![Organa awards Solo and Skywalker for their selflessness during the Battle of Yavin.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/Leia_honors_Han_and_Luke.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20151023234158)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/Leia_honors_Han_and_Luke.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151023234158) 

Organa awards Solo and Skywalker for their selflessness during the Battle of Yavin.

 

A rushed[[33]](#cite_note-Ultimate-33) [award ceremony](/wiki/Royal_Award_Ceremony "Royal Award Ceremony") was held later for the heroes of the battle, which included Solo. The three awardees, Solo, Skywalker and Chewbacca, walked the aisle past hundreds of Alliance personnel. They reached the stage, where Organa placed a [medal](/wiki/Medal_of_Bravery "Medal of Bravery") around Solo's neck as he winked at her. Skywalker was given his [medal](/wiki/Medal "Medal") and they bowed to the princess and turned as the crowd clapped for them.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-6) Organa delivered her speech, next. She asked them all to not forget the lives lost on Alderaan and during the battle, including her[[72]](#cite_note-Leia_1-72) adopted [parents](/wiki/Parent "Parent"),[[73]](#cite_note-Episode_III-73) [Viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy "Viceroy") [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") and [Queen](/wiki/Alderaanian_monarchy "Alderaanian monarchy") [Breha Organa](/wiki/Breha_Organa "Breha Organa"). Dodonna followed up by informing the base's population their next course of action: [evacuate Yavin 4](/wiki/Evacuation_of_Yavin_4 "Evacuation of Yavin 4"). The ceremony was adjourned. Organa playfully told Solo that he and his first mate had better get work.[[72]](#cite_note-Leia_1-72)
