Together they rescued Des and her team from the *Leviathan*'s tracks. Solo chastised Des for making a suicide run and told her not to do it unless there was no other choice. Solo was then informed Chewbacca was coming to help them finish off the *Leviathan*. Solo met up with Chewie at the base after Skywalker rescued him with information from Shu-Torun.[[112]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_41-112)

With the Patisans, Solo and the others made a plan to attack the *Leviathan* using the plans Chewie acquired. Solo agreed to fly the mission and keep an eye on the partisans. As the partisans boarded the *Falcon*, Solo and the others came under attack by stormtroopers. Benthic was wounded and Solo told partisans to get aboard the *Falcon* to escape. As the *Falcon* made its escape, Solo did not believe that Des should be leading the mission. Solo was reluctant to take the lead, but was convinced by Chewie to take charge since he was the *Falcon*'s captain. Solo saw that the *Leviathan*'s guns were down and led the partisans in attacking the stormtroopers stationed there.[[113]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_42-113)

Solo and the Partisans were able to make their way to the bridge. On the bridge, Solo, Leia, Des, and the partisans were able to pilot the *Leviathan* into Jedha City's crater. Solo ordered the Partisans to barricade the bridge to prevent the Empire from stopping their plans. Solo and the Partisans were able to return to the *Falcon* before it fell into the crater. Solo took the partisans back to NaJedha. Benthic told Solo that he and his fellow partisans would guard Jedha's ashes until it was gone. Before leaving, Solo awarded Des the Medal of Bravery for her actions, even though it was a copy.[[114]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_43-114)

#### Crait[]

From the captain's seat of the *Millennium Falcon*, Solo led the defense of the Rebel fleet from an [attack](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Rebel_fleet "Attack on the Rebel fleet") by Imperial forces, buying time for the fleet to jump to [Baraan-Fa](/wiki/Baraan-Fa "Baraan-Fa"). Shortly after, he accompanied [Wedge Antilles](/wiki/Wedge_Antilles "Wedge Antilles"), Leia, Luke, and Chewbacca on a [mission to Crait](/wiki/Mission_to_Crait "Mission to Crait"), which the Alliance was considering as a location for its hidden base of operations. There they met [Trusk Berinato](/wiki/Trusk_Berinato "Trusk Berinato"), an old ally of Bail Organa who Leia thought would help the Alliance. Instead Trusk had forged environmental reports and summoned SCAR Squadron to eliminate the Rebels. Solo attempted to evacuate Leia while Luke and Wedge engaged SCAR Squadron, but Trusk shot him in the shoulder. Leia returned fire, incapacitating Trusk as the Rebels regrouped and left the system aboard the *Millennium Falcon*.[[115]](#cite_note-Storms_of_Crait-115)

#### Mutiny on Mon Cala[]

Solo took Admiral [Gial Ackbar](/wiki/Gial_Ackbar "Gial Ackbar"), Skywalker, and Leia to Mon Cala. There, they met with Mon Cala's [Regent](/wiki/Regent "Regent"), [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Dors Urtya](/wiki/Dors_Urtya "Dors Urtya"). Ackbar and Leia asked Urtya for the [Mon Cala Mercantile Fleet](/wiki/Mon_Cala_Mercantile_Fleet "Mon Cala Mercantile Fleet") to become part of the Rebel Alliance's fleet. Solo spotted a [patrol transport](/wiki/LAAT/le_patrol_gunship "LAAT/le patrol gunship") approaching their position and came under attack. The transport landed, and Solo approached the troopers. Solo was able to bribe the sergeant and toss a detonator into the transport. Solo called to Chewie to bring up the boat so they could escape. Solo drove the boat past several creatures. Unfortunately, Urtya refused to give the Alliance the fleet, and Solo took Leia and Ackbar back to the [Mako-Ta Space Docks](/wiki/Mako-Ta_Space_Docks "Mako-Ta Space Docks"). There, he gave Skywalker a drink.[[116]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_44-116) In the mess hall, they met up with Wedge Antilles, ["Hobbie" Klivian](/wiki/Derek_Klivian "Derek Klivian"), and [Zev Senesca](/wiki/Zev_Senesca "Zev Senesca"). Together, they commemorated the fallen pilots of [Red Squadron](/wiki/Red_Squadron_(Galactic_Alliance) "Red Squadron (Galactic Alliance)").[[117]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_45-117)

Leia arrived in the hall with a mission. With Skywalker and Chewie, Solo went with Leia to [Dex Acquisitions Depot](/wiki/Dex_Acquisitions_Depot "Dex Acquisitions Depot") on [Meor Ain](/wiki/Meor_Ain "Meor Ain"). Together they broke into the depot's ultra-security brig and took the [Clawdite](/wiki/Clawdite "Clawdite") Tunga Arpagion with them[[117]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_45-117) aboard the *Falcon*. Solo and the others were able to convince him to pose as [Moff](/wiki/Moff "Moff") [Tan Hubi](/wiki/Tan_Hubi "Tan Hubi") while they used him to free [King](/wiki/King_of_Mon_Cala "King of Mon Cala") [Lee-Char](/wiki/Lee-Char "Lee-Char"). With Skywalker, Solo and Chewie were able to infiltrate the [Moncaladrome](/wiki/Moncaladrome "Moncaladrome") through the refresher. Posing as an attendant, Solo bluffed his way past a officer by allowing her to dry her hands on Chewie. Solo was then given a tip, much to Chewie's chagrin. They were able to take Moff Hubi and switch him with Tunga.[[118]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_46-118)

Solo flew a [submarine](/wiki/Submarine "Submarine") to [Strokill Prime](/wiki/Strokill_Prime "Strokill Prime") to rescue Lee-Char. Chewie was able to use Hubi's bio-signature to get past Strokill Prime's defenses, in addition to codes provided by Queen Trios.[[118]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_46-118) Solo flew the submarine past a [monstrous fish](/wiki/Opee_sea_killer "Opee sea killer"). Solo watched as Skywalker allowed the fish to swallow him. After Chewie rescued Skywalker from the fish, Solo took the submarine to the [Imperial base](/wiki/Unidentified_Imperial_base_(Strokill_Prime) "Unidentified Imperial base (Strokill Prime)") and docked inside it. Solo and Leia stunned several of the guards. Unfortunately, they discovered that the king was on life-support and could not be moved.[[119]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_47-119)

Solo and Skywalker argued about their next move. Solo and Skywalker searched for recording droid so Leia could deliver Lee-Char's words to his people. Solo found one and recorded Lee-Char's speech. After the guards killed Lee-Char, Solo and the others returned to the submarine to escape. On Mon Cala, Solo and the others met up with 3PO and [Tunga Arpagion](/wiki/Tunga_Arpagion "Tunga Arpagion"). They were confronted by Grand Admiral Urtya and several of his people who demanded Lee-Char's recording. After Urtya stunned Leia, Solo allowed him to take Lee-Char's recording. As Solo flew the *Falcon* away from Mon Cala, they were joined by the Mercantile fleet and a pair of Star Destroyers.[[120]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_48-120)

As the Empire sent in bombers to destroy the *Falcon* and the Mercantile fleet, Solo was contacted by Urtya, who agreed to rebel against the Empire. They were then joined by the Rebel Alliance fleet under Ackbar, that would protect the fleet. Solo told Leia to get into one of the *Falcon*'s turrets and destroy the bombers. Solo saw that the Empire was targeting the Mon Calamari's escape pods and took the *Falcon* to stop several TIEs before they could destroy the pods. After the *Aurora Flare* blew up and destroyed one of the Star Destroyers, Solo had the *Falcon* jump into hyperspace and escape with both the Rebel Alliance fleet and the mercantile fleet. Solo dropped Tunga off at the [Cosmatanic Steppes](/wiki/Cosmatanic_Steppes "Cosmatanic Steppes").[[121]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_49-121)

#### Escape from the Mako-Ta Space Docks[]

At the same time as a Rebel party to celebrate the expanded Rebel fleet at the Mako-Ta Space Docks, Solo, Chewie, and 3PO went to the [Ring of Kafrene](/wiki/Ring_of_Kafrene "Ring of Kafrene") to meet with an [Alaphani](/wiki/Alaphani "Alaphani") in a bar for a deal for a set of [transponder codes](/wiki/Transponder_code "Transponder code"). C-3PO translated the [Alaphani language](/wiki/Alaphani_(language) "Alaphani (language)") for Solo, and the deal went well. During the closing phases of the deal, Solo briefly joked about giving C-3PO to the Alaphani for 10 percent off. C-3PO was concerned by this, but Solo explained he was joking and that no Alaphani would accept that deal. Chewie then approached 3PO and Solo to alert them that two of Jabba the Hutt's bounty hunters were in the bar. After hearing this, Solo finished the deal, and the trio quickly left. The two bounty hunters followed, but Solo and Chewbacca hid behind their field of view to surprise them. Solo had C-3PO take the bounty hunters' weapons, and as the trio ran back to the *Falcon*, Solo yelled back and promised that Jabba would get his money.[[122]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_50-122)

C-3PO put the bounty hunters' weapons on the table on board, and Solo assured Chewbacca that they were not missing the party. He then explained to his partner that he had a contact who would pay them week for the set of codes. As the *Falcon* Chewie reminded Solo that Luke Skywalker had a role at the party, as he and other X-wing pilots planned to do a flyby for the gathered rebel allies. Solo admitted he would have liked to see it as well, and the *Falcon* left for the Space Docks.[[122]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_50-122) Solo arrived at the docks and found the Rebel fleet under attack by the Empire's [Death Squadron](/wiki/Death_Squadron "Death Squadron"). Leia said that Queen Trios had betrayed them and disabled all the cruisers and their hangar bays. Leia told Solo to fly into a bay door in order to open it. Solo, despite his better judgment, took the *Falcon* close to Star Destroyer and several TIEs following him as he made a run towards one of the cruisers. The *Falcon* then came under attack by Lord Vader in his [TIE Advanced](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_TIE_Advanced "Darth Vader's TIE Advanced").[[123]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_51-123)

Solo was able to evade Vader while Chewie tried to shoot him down. Solo flew the *Falcon* towards a [cruiser](/wiki/Lajaie%27s_cruiser "Lajaie's cruiser") as Vader fired several missiles at him. However, Vader was able to force the *Falcon* away from the cruiser's hangar doors. After Commander [Lajaie](/wiki/Lajaie "Lajaie")'s cruiser was destroyed, Solo decided to send a messenger to Leia by sending 3PO by escape pod. Solo flew the *Falcon* through the cruiser's debris, hoping Vader would not follow him. Chewie was able to launch 3PO to land on the [*Republic*](/wiki/Republic_(MC80A_Home_One_Type_Heavy_Star_Cruiser) "Republic (MC80A Home One Type Heavy Star Cruiser)").[[124]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_52-124) Solo received helped from Skywalker's newly formed [Rogue Squadron](/wiki/Rogue_Squadron "Rogue Squadron"). Solo led the squadron in taking out the TIEs.[[125]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_53-125)

Solo was forced to land the *Falcon* on Ackbar's cruiser after taking heavy damage from Vader.[[125]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_53-125) He then took a [Flight suit](/wiki/Flight_suit "Flight suit") and took an X-wing and rejoined the fight. Solo and Skywalker came across a TIE that was acting weird and realized that an ally was aboard. Solo and Skywalker led the TIE back to the cruiser. There, they learned that Leia was the pilot and got her to the *Republic*'s bridge. The *Republic* was able to escape into hyperspace.[[126]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_54-126) Solo, Skywalker, and the rest of Rogue Squadron returned to help the surviving cruisers. Solo defended Leia and Skywalker's ship as they boarded the base to rescue Mothma and the other ambassadors. During the retreat, Solo and R2's X-wing was damaged but was rescued by a rebel *Quasar Fire*-class carrier.[[127]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_55-127)

As the carrier went into hyperspace, it engines were fried and cruiser had to land on [Corosi 7](/wiki/Corosi_7 "Corosi 7"). Solo was unable to contact Ackbar or Chewie due to the Rebel fleet being kept hidden throughout the Outer Rim. Despite that, Solo was then given a promotion to the rank of [colonel](/wiki/Colonel "Colonel") by Mothma, though he refused it. Solo then came up with plan to find Chewie and the *Falcon*. Solo took Leia and Skywalker to Nar Shadaa to meet with Starros, who agreed to help them.[[127]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_55-127)

Starros was forced to drop them off on [Hubin](/wiki/Hubin "Hubin"), where they were stranded for weeks.[[128]](#cite_note-SW_56-128) They eventually stole a shuttle when SCAR Squadron arrived. The team then hunted the remaining rebels and arrived at the [Kaliida Nebula](/wiki/Kaliida_Nebula "Kaliida Nebula") and met *Home One*.[[129]](#cite_note-SW_61-129)

Later, Organa came up with a plan to destabilize Shu-Torun's industry. She recruited her team, the tech [Meorti](/wiki/Meorti "Meorti"), actor Tunga Arpagion, and the Partisans to pose as Queen Trios and disrupt the [Spike](/wiki/Spike_(Shu-Torun) "Spike (Shu-Torun)").[[130]](#cite_note-SW_62-130)

#### Investigating Lotho Minor[]

:   "*And I'm not giving up on this planet yet.*"
:   ―Leia Organa[[131]](#cite_note-The_Planet_of_Misfit_Droids-131)

Han, Leia, Luke, Chewbacca, and C-3PO, were sent by the Alliance to Restore the Republic to investigate the planet [Lotho Minor](/wiki/Lotho_Minor "Lotho Minor") for a new base. During the investigation, they ran into native droids and a male [Duros](/wiki/Duros "Duros") named [Akar Duel](/wiki/Akar_Duel "Akar Duel"). Their actions drove Han and the rest from Lotho Minor knowing that the planet was not a good location for a new rebel base.[[131]](#cite_note-The_Planet_of_Misfit_Droids-131)

#### Rebel duty on Hoth[]

:   "*Listen sweetheart, I'm no hero. I saw a fight and pointed my ship at it.*"
:   ―Solo's response to [Corwi Selgrothe](/wiki/Corwi_Selgrothe "Corwi Selgrothe") asking what the Rebellion meant to him[[132]](#cite_note-Heroes-132)

 [![Solo converses with Threepio while repairing the Falcon alongside Chewie in Echo Base.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/Han_Threepio_R2_Chewie_Falcon_in_Echo_base.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180119054546) [![Solo converses with Threepio while repairing the Falcon alongside Chewie in Echo Base.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/Han_Threepio_R2_Chewie_Falcon_in_Echo_base.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/280?cb=20180119054546)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/Han_Threepio_R2_Chewie_Falcon_in_Echo_base.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180119054546) 

Solo converses with Threepio while repairing the *Falcon* alongside Chewie in Echo Base.

 

Over three years after the Death Star's destruction at Skywalker's hand at the Battle of Yavin, the Alliance established a new base in the [Anoat sector](/wiki/Anoat_sector "Anoat sector") on the ice planet [Hoth](/wiki/Hoth "Hoth"), far from the Empire's reach.[[133]](#cite_note-Echo_Base_Databank-133) The base was aptly designated [Echo Base](/wiki/Echo_Base "Echo Base"), as it was carved into the rocky caverns of the [Clabburn Range](/wiki/Clabburn_Range "Clabburn Range") of mountains. Within months of the new base being established, Solo, Organa, Skywalker, and the others of Organa's team were deployed by Rebel High Command to Hoth aboard the *Falcon*.[[134]](#cite_note-Episode_V_Episode_Guide-134) Solo and Skywalker scouted out the land around the base on regular recon missions as a part of their duties, using reptilian [tauntauns](/wiki/Tauntaun "Tauntaun") as mounts to better traverse the freezing landscape.[[75]](#cite_note-Absolutely_Everything-75)

Solo took well to mounting and riding the unruly tauntauns and was sent on a reconnaissance mission in order to locate a ship that had gone missing a month before during a snow storm. The deflector shield which protected Echo Base from attack had been damaged and made inoperative, and the equipment aboard the lost ship was needed to repair the shield's generator. At dawn, Solo, Organa, and the rebel veteran Twi'lek General [Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Hera_Syndulla "Hera Syndulla") ventured into the frigid mountains in search of the lost ship. Throughout the day, however, Solo and Syndulla mastered tauntaun riding, while Organa had trouble controlling her beast and—to Solo's amusement—was de-[saddled](/wiki/Saddle "Saddle"). While Solo helped the Princess re-mount her tauntaun, he informed the search team that night was fast approaching and they would soon have to return to Echo Base empty-handed. For her part, Organa insisted they couldn't return without first finding the lost ship. As she spoke, Organa again lost control of her tauntaun and stumbled backwards and fell from a steep embankment into a pit. Panicked, Solo and Syndulla rushed to the cliff edge and were relieved to see the princess unharmed, having literally stumbled across the lost Rebel ship at the bottom of the pit. Solo and Syndulla made their way safely to the bottom of the pit, arriving at Organa's position minutes later, and learned that Organa had found the equipment that could be used to repair the shield generator, and had fought off a massive carnivorous [wampa](/wiki/Wampa "Wampa"). The trio then returned to Echo Base victorious.[[135]](#cite_note-Forces_of_Destiny_Leia-135)

 [![Solo took well to riding tauntauns on Hoth.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/HanTauntaun-TESB40.png/revision/latest?cb=20211226005528) [![Solo took well to riding tauntauns on Hoth.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/HanTauntaun-TESB40.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20211226005528)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/HanTauntaun-TESB40.png/revision/latest?cb=20211226005528) 

Solo took well to riding tauntauns on Hoth.

 

At some point, Solo and his allies ran into the bounty hunter[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21) [Skorr](/wiki/Skorr "Skorr")[[136]](#cite_note-Whills_Strike_Back-136) on [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell "Ord Mantell"). The encounter convinced him to leave and fulfill his debt to Jabba, so he began repairing the *Falcon* on Hoth. Believing himself to be leaving, he, after scouting around the frozen wastes of Hoth with Skywalker under the callsign [Echo Seven](/wiki/Echo_Seven "Echo Seven"), had a heated conversation with Leia, claiming that she had romantic feelings towards him. After this debate, Solo learned Luke had gone missing on patrol. Riding out on[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21) a tauntaun named [Murra](/wiki/Murra_(tauntaun) "Murra (tauntaun)")[[137]](#cite_note-FACPOV_She_will_keep_them_warm-137) in the midst of snowstorm, Han found Luke had been attacked by a wampa.[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21)

After Murra collapsed[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21) and died from the cold,[[138]](#cite_note-Hasbro_Han_Hoth-138) Han used Luke's lightsaber to cut the animal open and placed him inside to prevent him from freezing to death. After bringing Luke back to recover from his injuries, Han and Chewbacca went out to investigate a signal and encountered an [Imperial probe droid](/wiki/XJ9-CS14 "XJ9-CS14"). Realizing the Empire had discovered their location, the Rebels decided to evacuate. During the [ensuing battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Hoth "Battle of Hoth"), Han rescued Leia from the collapsed command center, leading her towards her transport. A tunnel collapse cut off their way there, so Han, Chewie, Leia, and C-3PO escaped on the still-unrepaired *Falcon*.[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21)

#### On the run from the Empire[]

:   "*What are you doing? You're not actually going into an asteroid field?*"  
    "*They'd be crazy to follow us, wouldn't they?*"
:   ―Princess Leia Organa and Han Solo[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21)

 [![Han and Leia share a kiss aboard the Millennium Falcon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Hanleiafalcon.png/revision/latest?cb=20130324024232) [![Han and Leia share a kiss aboard the Millennium Falcon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Hanleiafalcon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20130324024232)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cd/Hanleiafalcon.png/revision/latest?cb=20130324024232) 

Han and Leia share a kiss aboard the *Millennium Falcon*.

 

In space, the *Falcon* was pursued by several Star Destroyers and TIE fighters. While Solo was working on repairs, the ship drifted into an [asteroid field](/wiki/Hoth_asteroid_field "Hoth asteroid field"). Claiming that the Imperials would be "crazy" to follow them, Solo flew into the asteroid field, which would cause extensive damage to the pursuing Imperial Fleet. After the immediately pursuing TIE fighters were destroyed by asteroids, Solo landed the *Falcon* in a cave on a large asteroid, where he continued to work on repairs. While repairing the *Falcon*, Han and Leia shared a kiss before being interrupted by C-3PO.[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21)

Inside the cave, Leia saw something outside the ship, so she, Han, and Chewbacca went out to investigate. Discovering that [mynocks](/wiki/Mynock "Mynock") were the cause, Chewbacca accidentally fired a shot into the cave, which caused a tremor. Solo realized something wasn't right; he fired his blaster into the ground, causing another tremor. The three returned to the *Falcon*, flying out of the cave, which they discovered was actually the inside of an [exogorth](/wiki/Exogorth "Exogorth") slug[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21) named [Sy-O](/wiki/Sy-O "Sy-O"). Although Sy-O attempted to keep them inside the internal ecosystem of itself by closing its mouth, the *Falcon* escaped, with Solo and the others never knowing Sy-O had loved them as friends despite their brief stay.[[139]](#cite_note-This_Is_No_Cave-139) Fleeing back towards the Imperials, Solo flew straight towards the bridge of the Star Destroyer *Avenger*, then hid on the back of the bridge. The ruse worked; the Imperials were unable to find the ship. Preparing to spread about the galaxy to search for the *Falcon*, the Imperial fleet dumped its trash, and Solo detached the *Falcon*, which floated off with the rest of the trash. Solo then decided to go to [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City "Cloud City"), a [tibanna](/wiki/Tibanna "Tibanna") gas mine on [Bespin](/wiki/Bespin "Bespin") run by his old friend Lando Calrissian. Unknown to the rebels, however, Boba Fett had also hidden his ship, the *[Slave I](/wiki/Slave_I "Slave I")*, among the Empire's trash, and followed them to Cloud City.[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21)

#### Imprisonment in carbonite[]

:   "*I love you."  
    "I know.*"
:   ―Leia Organa and Han Solo[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21)

 [![Han Solo greets Lando Calrissian on Cloud City.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Hansolo10.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091202150611) [![Han Solo greets Lando Calrissian on Cloud City.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Hansolo10.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20091202150611)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Hansolo10.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091202150611) 

Han Solo greets Lando Calrissian on Cloud City.

 

On Cloud City, Han met his old friend Lando Calrissian, who despite showing initial hostility, embraced his old friend. Calrissian provided the rebels with lodging and promised to repair the *Falcon*. While Han said he didn't trust Lando, due to his knowledge of Calrissian being a scoundrel, he appeared to be at ease in Cloud City, while Leia felt suspicious due to C-3PO going missing and then reappearing in pieces. Calrissian then invited Solo, Organa, and Chewbacca for refreshments, and told them about a deal that would keep the Empire out of Cloud City. To Solo's surprise, he led them into a room with Darth Vader. Solo immediately drew his blaster and fired several shots at the Sith Lord, but Vader blocked the shots and pulled the blaster out of Solo's hands with the Force.[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21)

Solo was then tortured by the Empire, but he claimed they didn't even ask him any questions. When placed in a cell, Calrissian arrived and told the prisoners that Solo would be handed over to Fett, who would take him to Jabba, and that they were a trap set by Vader for Han and Leia's friend Luke Skywalker. Angrily, Solo attacked his "friend", but was restrained.[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21)

Vader planned to take Skywalker to his master, [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), by encasing him in [carbonite](/wiki/Carbonite "Carbonite"). Unsure if a human could survive the process, he decided to test it on Solo. Tearfully, Leia confessed her love to Han, to which he simply replied that he knew. Leia, Chewbacca, Calrissian, Fett, and Vader looked on as Han was lowered into the carbon-freezing chamber and frozen. He survived the freezing process and fell into hibernation. He was then handed over to Fett and loaded onto *Slave I*. Despite a rescue attempt by Leia, Lando, and Chewie, Fett escaped Cloud City, taking the frozen form of Han Solo with him.[[21]](#cite_note-Episode_V-21)

#### Stolen by Qi'ra[]

:   "*They all love him. Hate him. Need him. Owe him or are owed* by *him. Han Solo unites the galaxy. And that, right now, is* exactly *what I need. Han always wanted to save me. Now he'll get his chance.*"
:   ―Lady Qi'ra, to Margo[[140]](#cite_note-SW:_WOTBH_1-140)

Due to the instability of the carbonite freezing process, Han began to melt aboard *Slave I*, forcing Fett to make an emergency landing on Nar Shaddaa. He met with [Doc Ragon](/wiki/Ragon "Ragon"), a doctor with whom Fett had a history, and the [Besalisk](/wiki/Besalisk "Besalisk") tasked Fett with killing [Wyrmen Lictor](/wiki/Wyrmen_Lictor "Wyrmen Lictor") in exchange for his help. As he fought against various [pit](/wiki/Fighting_pit "Fighting pit") warriors, Doc managed to halt the melting and keep Han alive. However, he was then killed by a group of assailants who took Han and left Nar Shaddaa.[[141]](#cite_note-SW:_WOTBH_A_1-141) After securing Han, they arrived at the [*Vermillion*](/wiki/Vermillion_(Crimson_Dawn) "Vermillion (Crimson Dawn)"), where he was delivered to the reformed Crimson Dawn and its new leader, Qi'ra, who intended to use Solo to lure together major galactic players for her [own plans](/wiki/War_against_the_Sith "War against the Sith"). With Han in her custody, Qi'ra sent out a message to various factions in the criminal underworld, inviting them to an [auction](/wiki/Auction_for_Han_Solo "Auction for Han Solo") on [Jekara](/wiki/Jekara "Jekara"). After delivering the message, Qi'ra then explained to her associate [Margo](/wiki/Margo "Margo") that Han was directly connected to almost every powerful faction in the galaxy. Thus, he would be useful to both her and Crimson Dawn.[[140]](#cite_note-SW:_WOTBH_1-140) Still, Qi'ra fully intended for Solo to end up back with the Rebellion and ensured his location was leaked to agent [Amilyn Holdo](/wiki/Amilyn_Holdo "Amilyn Holdo"). She also placed a tracker on his carbonite slab.[[142]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2020_18-142)

Once the representatives of the various syndicates arrived, Qi'ra thanked them for coming as she introduced herself and officially announced Crimson Dawn's return. She then revealed Han to the crowd and started the bidding at one hundred thousand credits. After multiple bids from different parties, the present members of the Hutt Clan began to bid over one another with increasingly higher offers. But this soon ended when Jabba bid with one million credits. With no other bids, Qi'ra congratulated Jabba and told him that the smuggler was his. However, the auction was then interrupted by the arrival of Darth Vader. Guarded by death troopers, Vader declared that Han belonged to him, to which Qi'ra smiled and decided to see where this would go.[[143]](#cite_note-War_of_the_Bounty_Hunters_2-143) After Jabba conceded his ownership of Han to the Sith Lord, Qi'ra briefly [sparred](/wiki/Duel_on_the_Vermillion "Duel on the Vermillion") with Vader before being knocked into Han and incapacitated. But before Vader could kill Qi'ra, he suddenly sensed Luke's presence through the Force.[[144]](#cite_note-War_of_the_Bounty_Hunters_3-144) After establishing communication with Luke's X-wing, Vader informed him that he had Han in his possession. He then warned his son that if he did not come to him, then he would cut his friend in half.[[145]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_16_(2020)-145) But Luke refused and told Vader to come to him instead. Vader conceded, ordering General [Romodi](/wiki/Hurst_Romodi "Hurst Romodi") to bring Han aboard his star destroyer and prepare his fighter.[[146]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_16_(2020)-146) Han was then loaded onto an Imperial shuttle before it took off from Jekara.[[147]](#cite_note-War_of_the_Bounty_Hunters_4-147)

After being brought aboard the *Executor*, Han was transported to the ship's detention level under heavy guard. However, a surprise attack from the Hutt fleet allowed Leia, Lando and Chewbacca to infiltrate Vader's flagship and eliminate the stormtroopers guarding Han. But before they could escape with him, they were once again intercepted by Fett. One of the Hutt ships then blasted a hole in the room they were in, causing Han to be sucked out into space. Utilizing his jetpack, Fett pursued Han all the way down to the surface of Jekara. He then fished Han up[[148]](#cite_note-War_of_the_Bounty_Hunters_5-148) before he hit the sea[[142]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2020_18-142) and returned him to *Slave I* before flying him to Tatooine, fighting off IG-88[[149]](#cite_note-WotBH-IG-88_1-149) and finally turning him in to Jabba. Though Fett suggested dumping Han into the [Great Pit of Carkoon](/wiki/Great_Pit_of_Carkoon "Great Pit of Carkoon"), Jabba ultimately decided to put the smuggler on display in his palace.[[148]](#cite_note-War_of_the_Bounty_Hunters_5-148)

### Rescue and marriage[]

#### Rescue from Jabba[]

##### Prelude[]

:   "*Over and over, he fought and risked his life and sacrificed and personally saved the entire* Alliance *more than once. He stayed because even if he couldn't admit it, even to himself, he* believes *in this cause. Han Solo's a smuggler because he likes it, but he's a rebel because he's Han Solo. And Han Solo complains and jokes and is generally half-useless…but he doesn't leave. That's inspiring. He* matters*. To the Rebellion…and to me.*"
:   ―Leia Organa, on Han Solo[[150]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_(2020)_12-150)

Through her tracker, Qi'ra learned that Solo had been brought to Jabba's Palace and discovered he had been placed on the Hutt's wall as a decoration. Traveling to the *Millennium Falcon*, where everyone aboard believed Solo had died in the fall to Jekara, Qi'ra revealed Solo's survival and imprisonment in Jabba's Palace. Organa agreed to wait for Qi'ra to confirm the time was right to launch a rescue operation, knowing she was needed with the Alliance and could not spend time on a rescue mission at the moment. Qi'ra promised to reach out, even arguing that Solo would be safe in Jabba's Palace while the rebels waged their war with the Empire,[[142]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_2020_18-142) but Crimson Dawn would be destroyed in the [Battle at Amaxine Station](/wiki/Battle_at_Amaxine_Station "Battle at Amaxine Station").[[151]](#cite_note-Hidden_Empire_5-151)

Later, the Rebel Alliance began preparations for the mission. Leia, Chewbacca, and R2-D2 sought the help of Maz Kanata, but were forced into a brief skirmish with the [Ubese](/wiki/Ubese "Ubese") bounty hunter [Boushh](/wiki/Boushh "Boushh"). After quickly overpowering him, Leia took his clothes, helmet, and thermal detonator as a disguise to sneak into Jabba's palace.[[152]](#cite_note-Bounty_Hunted-152)

##### The rescue[]

:   "*Victims of the almighty sarlacc: His Excellency hopes that you will die honorably. But should any of you wish to beg for mercy, the great Jabba the Hutt will now listen to your pleas.*"  
    "*Threepio, you tell that slimy piece of worm-ridden filth he'll get no such pleasure from us. Right?*"
:   ―C-3PO, translating for Jabba the Hutt, and Han Solo[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-15)

 [![Han freed from the carbonite by Leia](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Hibernation_sickness.png/revision/latest?cb=20130331020628) [![Han freed from the carbonite by Leia](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Hibernation_sickness.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130331020628)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Hibernation_sickness.png/revision/latest?cb=20130331020628) 

Han freed from the carbonite by Leia

 

After almost a full year in captivity,[[36]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-36) Solo was released from the carbonite by Leia, disguised as the bounty hunter Boushh. Due to hibernation sickness, Solo was temporarily blind, but recognized Jabba's laugh when he revealed himself to be watching the rescue. Solo was then placed in a prison cell with his partner Chewbacca, while Leia was taken as a personal slave by Jabba. After Leia was captured, Luke Skywalker arrived, and faced off against Jabba's prized Rancor, killing it. In rage, Jabba sentenced Skywalker, Solo, and the Wookiee to be fed to the [sarlacc](/wiki/Sarlacc "Sarlacc") in the Great Pit of Carkoon.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-15)

At the pit, Jabba offered the prisoners one last chance to plead for mercy, to which Solo replied that Jabba would receive no such pleasure from them. Skywalker then offered Jabba one last chance to free them, which he denied. R2-D2 then released [Luke's lightsaber](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker%27s_green_lightsaber "Luke Skywalker's green lightsaber"); Luke caught it and began a battle. In the ensuing struggle, Han was still mostly blind, rendering him unable to contribute much. However, after being told by Chewbacca that Boba Fett had joined the battle, Han unintentionally swung an axe into Fett's jetpack, sending him flying into Jabba's sail barge and then rolling into the sarlacc. After a blaster shot knocked Lando, disguised as a palace guard, off the skiff they were on, Han lowered the axe for Lando to grab, but Calrissian's foot was caught by one of the sarlacc's tentacles. Claiming his vision had "gotten a lot better," Han shot the tentacle and pulled Lando back up into the skiff. Luke then rescued Leia, Artoo, and Threepio from the sail barge and destroyed it, and then the rebels escaped.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-15)

#### The Battle of Endor[]

:   "*I love you."  
    "I know.*"
:   ―Han Solo and Leia Organa during the Battle of Endor[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-15)

 [![Solo on Endor](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/HanEndor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080329135130) [![Solo on Endor](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/HanEndor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20080329135130)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/eb/HanEndor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080329135130) 

Solo on Endor

 

After being rescued, Han joined the Alliance and was given the rank of General. As part of the attack on the [second Death Star](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station"), with Skywalker, Organa, and Chewbacca, Han commandeered the *[Tydirium](/wiki/Tydirium "Tydirium")*, a captured Imperial shuttle, and took a Rebel strike team to the forest moon of Endor to disable the shields protecting the superweapon. Shortly after landing on the forest moon, the strike team encountered a group of [scout troopers](/wiki/Scout_trooper "Scout trooper"). Solo attempted to sneak up on them, but failed to do so, alerting them and allowing two to escape. Luke and Leia hopped on a speeder to pursue them, leaving Solo and the rest of the strike team behind.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-15)

Luke eventually made his way back to the rest of the Rebels, without information on Leia. Luke, Han, Chewie, Artoo, and Threepio set off to find Leia, while Han sent the rest of the strike team to move towards the shield generator. While looking, the rebels came across[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-15) a [verkle](/wiki/Verkle "Verkle") trap[[153]](#cite_note-Geektionary-153) laid by the native [Ewoks](/wiki/Ewok "Ewok"). Despite Solo urging him to ignore the dead animal,[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-15) the verkle's smell ended up being irresistible to Chewbacca,[[153]](#cite_note-Geektionary-153) who triggered the trap. Upon releasing the rebels, the furry tribesmen believed C-3PO to be a god, and they attempted to cook the others at a banquet in his honor. However, Luke used the Force to levitate the "god" in a demonstration of his "magic", frightening the Ewoks into releasing the others. At the village, the Rebels found Leia, and C-3PO managed to befriend the Ewoks. Luke then left the other rebels to confront his father, Darth Vader.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-15)

 [![Han Solo with Leia Organa after the Battle of Endor](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/Han_and_Leia_on_Endor.png/revision/latest?cb=20160320032434) [![Han Solo with Leia Organa after the Battle of Endor](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/Han_and_Leia_on_Endor.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20160320032434)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/Han_and_Leia_on_Endor.png/revision/latest?cb=20160320032434) 

Han Solo with Leia Organa after the Battle of Endor

 

The next day, Solo's group met up with the main Rebel strike team at the shield generator, but Ewok scouts informed them of a less-guarded rear entrance. After three of the four guards were distracted by the Ewok [Paploo](/wiki/Paploo "Paploo"), the Rebels neutralized the last guard and entered the shield bunker. But the operation proved to be a trap, and Solo and the Rebels were captured. However, the Empire had not expected the Ewoks to attack, which allowed the Rebels to escape. For most of the battle, Han stayed at the door, trying to open it. After R2-D2 was damaged while attempting to open it, Han unsuccessfully tried to hotwire the door open. He then impersonated the pilot of an AT-ST that had been captured by Chewbacca and two Ewoks, getting the Imperials to open the doors. Han was then able to place detonators inside the shield generator, destroying it and leaving the Death Star vulnerable to attack. Han and Leia witnessed the Death Star's destruction, and she revealed to him that Luke was her brother. Solo participated with the other Rebels and Ewoks in the victory celebration held that night.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-15)

#### Aftermath of the battle[]

Following the battle, Solo, Chewbacca, and R2-D2 were sent by Organa to [General Syndulla's camp](/wiki/General_Syndulla%27s_camp "General Syndulla's camp") to obtain food rations for the Ewoks as a means to keep the furry creatures from making a meal out of the captured stormtroopers. While at Syndulla's camp, Syndulla forced Solo to admit that her ship the *[Ghost](/wiki/Ghost "Ghost")* was superior to the *Falcon* in order to get the rations.[[154]](#cite_note-AIF-154)

The morning after the Battle of Endor, Solo led the Pathfinders on an [assault](/wiki/Assault_on_an_Imperial_outpost "Assault on an Imperial outpost") on an [Imperial outpost](/wiki/Imperial_outpost_(Endor) "Imperial outpost (Endor)") on the far side of Endor. Knowing that the Imperial outpost was preparing for a counterattack, the rebel commanders dispatched Han Solo on a mission to destroy the base. Han outlined a plan for the Pathfinders and their Ewok allies to strike the outpost with limited air cover. During the assault, the rebel pilot Lieutenant [Shara Bey](/wiki/Shara_Bey "Shara Bey") served as the transport's pilot. The Pathfinders quickly wiped out the garrison, and Solo uncovered a lot of data in the outpost's computers, which led him to conclude that the war was not over.[[16]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_1-16)

Two days after the Battle of Endor, Solo proposed to Organa, who accepted the [marriage proposal](/wiki/Wedding_of_Han_Solo_and_Leia_Organa "Wedding of Han Solo and Leia Organa"). While in the Bright Tree Village,[[36]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-36) Han and Leia were then married; their ceremony was attended by only people they trusted.[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31) Solo and Organa departed Endor to have their honeymoon on the luxury [Star Cruiser](/wiki/Star_Cruiser "Star Cruiser") known as the *[Halcyon](/wiki/Halcyon "Halcyon")*, where they encountered an Imperial force. She also told him she had met Qi'ra, much to his surprise.[[36]](#cite_note-Princess_and_Scoundrel-36) As a wedding gift to his wife, Solo reconfigured some of the crew quarters on the *Falcon* to include a galley.[[155]](#cite_note-Cross-155)

### New Republic[]

#### Honoring a life debt[]

##### Gathering intelligence[]

Before the formal establishment of the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), Solo, C-3PO, and the Pathfinders participated in a [raid](/wiki/Raid_at_the_Wretch_of_Tayron "Raid at the Wretch of Tayron") on an ISB black site at the [Wretch](/wiki/Wretch_of_Tayron "Wretch of Tayron") of [Tayron](/wiki/Tayron "Tayron"). During the assault, the Pathfinders managed to down an AT-ST walker, which caused a breach in the facility's hall. This allowed Solo and his men to enter the base and secure the computers before the [base commander](/wiki/Unidentified_Imperial_base_commander "Unidentified Imperial base commander") could initiate a purge of the computers. With the aid of C-3PO, the Pathfinders were able to hack into the Imperial data files and discovered that the Empire had begun to execute [Operation: Cinder](/wiki/Operation:_Cinder "Operation: Cinder"), a posthumous order issued by the Emperor to devastate several worlds including [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") as retribution for his demise.[[156]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_3-156) The Pathfinders' actions enabled the Rebel Alliance to deploy forces to halt Operation: Cinder, saving many lives and worlds.[[157]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_4-157)

 [![Han Solo talks to Maz Kanata on Takodana.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/HanSoloTakodana.png/revision/latest?cb=20171123210917) [![Han Solo talks to Maz Kanata on Takodana.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/HanSoloTakodana.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20171123210917)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/HanSoloTakodana.png/revision/latest?cb=20171123210917) 

Han Solo talks to Maz Kanata on Takodana.

 

Several months after the Battle of Endor, Han arrived at Maz Kanata's castle on Takodana to rendezvous with an Imperial defector named [Ralsius Paldora](/wiki/Ralsius_Paldora "Ralsius Paldora"), who had stolen intelligence crucial to the liberation of Kashyyyk. The Empire had quickly discovered his treachery and followed him. Recovering the data cubes and fighting their way back to the *Falcon*, Han and Ralsius were [saved](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Takodana "Skirmish on Takodana") by the arrival of [Inferno Squad](/wiki/Inferno_Squad "Inferno Squad"), buying them time to escape the planet.[[158]](#cite_note-Battlefront_2-158)

##### False leads[]

:   "*C'mon, Chewie. Set new coordinates. It's time to get you home.*"
:   ―Han Solo to Chewbacca, on the way to liberate Kashyyyk[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18)

Some time later, Han and Chewbacca received additional intelligence from the smuggler [Imra](/wiki/Imra "Imra") that the Wookiee homeworld of [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk") would have a decreased Imperial presence.[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18) Against the advice of his wife, Leia, the two friends gathered several fellow smugglers and people who owed them favors for a [hastily planned campaign to liberate](/wiki/Liberation_of_Kashyyyk "Liberation of Kashyyyk") the planet. However, this turned out to be disinformation from the Empire to lure Han and his companions into a trap.[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

While Chewie attempted to board a gunship captained by the Wookiee [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") [Kirratha](/wiki/Kirratha "Kirratha"), they were attacked by two Star Destroyers and several TIE fighters. The Imperials disabled Kirratha's engines, leaving Chewie and Kirratha stranded in space. Han managed to escape, but Chewbacca was captured and locked in an Imperial prison called [Ashmead's Lock](/wiki/Ashmead%27s_Lock "Ashmead's Lock"). While traveling through the edge of [Wild Space](/wiki/Wild_Space "Wild Space"), Han contacted his wife to discuss the recent developments. However, he came under attack from Imperial forces and lost communication with Leia.[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

Princess Leia was unable to get help from the New Republic since they were preoccupied with fighting against the Galactic Empire. Since Han had resigned his commission as general in the [New Republic Defense Force](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Force "New Republic Defense Force"), he was low on their list of priorities. Desperate, Leia turned to the New Republic starfighter pilot [Norra Wexley](/wiki/Norra_Wexley "Norra Wexley") for help. Norra and Captain Wedge Antilles traveled to Solo's last known coordinates in Wild Space but found themselves under attack by Imperial forces. After being rescued by the New Republic Starfleet, Norra resigned her commission in the Starfleet to find Solo out of respect for Princess Leia.[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

##### Finding new allies[]

Norra, her son [Temmin Wexley](/wiki/Temmin_Wexley "Temmin Wexley"), his battle droid [Mister Bones](/wiki/Mister_Bones "Mister Bones"), the [Zabrak](/wiki/Zabrak "Zabrak") bounty hunter [Jas Emari](/wiki/Jas_Emari "Jas Emari"), the former Imperial [loyalty officer](/wiki/Loyalty_officer "Loyalty officer") [Sinjir Rath Velus](/wiki/Sinjir_Rath_Velus "Sinjir Rath Velus"), and the New Republic soldier [Jom Barell](/wiki/Jom_Barell "Jom Barell") traveled to the planet [Irudiru](/wiki/Irudiru "Irudiru") after learning that Solo had last been sighted at [Warrin Station](/wiki/Warrin_Station "Warrin Station"). There, they found Solo while scouting the compound of the [Siniteen](/wiki/Siniteen "Siniteen") prison designer [Golas Aram](/wiki/Golas_Aram "Golas Aram"). At a nearby [cantina](/wiki/Cantina "Cantina"), Solo informed his allies that he had discovered that Chewbacca was being held at Ashmead's Lock and that Aram was responsible for designing the prison. During their initial encounter, Solo was accosted by Mister Bones, who mistook him for a threat.[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

Working together, Solo and Norra's team managed to breach the compound and capture Aram. Under duress, Aram told the rebels how to enter Ashmead's Lock. However, he omitted the password that would allow them unhindered passage inside the prison. Traveling to the Kashyyyk system in the *Millennium Falcon* and Emari's ship *[Halo](/wiki/Halo "Halo")*, Solo and Norra's team gained clearance to land at Ashmead's Lock by claiming to be a repair team. Upon entering the prison, Han and the rebels were accosted by the prison's computer security system [SOL-GDA](/wiki/Synthesized_Operating_Layer,_Grid-Based_Drive_Array "Synthesized Operating Layer, Grid-Based Drive Array"), which dispatched droids to integrate them.[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

Temmin discovered that the prison was being powered by the prisoners who were being housed inside stasis cells. Using this information, Han and Norra managed to disable the power generator. As a result, Han and Norra's team were able to free Chewbacca and a hundred other prisoners including Norra's husband and Temmin's father [Brentin Lore Wexley](/wiki/Brentin_Lore_Wexley "Brentin Lore Wexley"). While Norra, Temmin, and Mister Bones took the liberated prisoners back to Chandrila on the *Falcon*, Han stayed behind with Chewbacca, Jas, Sinjir, and Jom to complete their mission to liberate the Wookiees. Unknown to Han and his allies, the Imperial [Fleet Admiral](/wiki/Fleet_Admiral "Fleet Admiral") [Gallius Rax](/wiki/Gallius_Rax "Gallius Rax") had inserted inorganic bio-chip implants inside the prisoners as part of a [plot](/wiki/Attack_on_Chandrila "Attack on Chandrila") to assassinate the New Republic leadership.[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

##### Liberating Kashyyyk[]

Han and his team learned that [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") [Lozen Tolruck](/wiki/Lozen_Tolruck "Lozen Tolruck") had fitted all of the Wookiees on Kashyyyk with [inhibitor chips](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip"). Tolruck controlled these inhibitor chips with a control module which he kept on his person. For the next month, Han and his team spent their time searching for Tolruck's island fortress and gathering Wookiee exiles and smugglers for a mass uprising. On one mission, Jom Barell was captured by Tolruck's forces and imprisoned at his [island fortress](/wiki/Lozen_Tolruck%27s_island_fortress "Lozen Tolruck's island fortress"). While Sinjir entered the island fortress to free Jom and disabled Tolruck's control module, Han and his team disabled the deflector shield generator at [Camp Sardo](/wiki/Camp_Sardo "Camp Sardo"). Despite being attacked by Imperial forces, Jas managed to take out the shield generator.[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

After Sinjir disabled Tolruck's control module, a mass planetwide Wookiee uprising broke out. The Wookiees and their rebel allies quickly overwhelmed the outnumbered Imperial garrison. When the orbiting Imperial Star Destroyers began bombarding Kashyyyk, Han, Chewbacca, and their fellow rebels managed to evacuate the civilians underground. They then took a ship loaded with [webweaver](/wiki/Webweaver "Webweaver") [spiders](/wiki/Spider "Spider") aboard the Star Destroyer *[Dominion](/wiki/Dominion "Dominion")* and fought their way through the ship's corridors. However, they were captured by stormtroopers who brought them before [Vice Admiral](/wiki/Vice_Admiral "Vice Admiral") [Domm Korgale](/wiki/Domm_Korgale "Domm Korgale").[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

Before the admiral could eliminate Han and his team, New Republic reinforcements arrived in the Kashyyyk system in the form of Leia and the *Millennium Falcon*, Antilles' Phantom Squadron, and Admiral Ackbar's flagship, *[Home One](/wiki/Home_One "Home One")*. Han and Chewbacca managed to break free of their captors and seize control of the *Dominion*. Han and his team then turned the ship's guns on the Star Destroyer *[Vitiator](/wiki/Vitiator "Vitiator")*. As a result, the remaining Star Destroyer *Neutralizer* surrendered to Admiral Ackbar.[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

Following the battle, Han and Leia experienced an emotional reunion aboard the *Dominion*. Returning to Kashyyyk, Han, Chewbacca, and Leia learned about the Liberation Day attacks on Chandrila. With the Wookiees undertaking mop-up operations against the remaining Imperial holdouts on Kashyyyk, Han insisted that Chewbacca stay behind and reunite with his [family](/wiki/Chewbacca%27s_family "Chewbacca's family"). However, he told Chewbacca that he would return if he ever needed help. Han then left Kashyyyk aboard the *Falcon* with Leia and their unborn child, [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo").[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

#### Balancing family and duty[]

Over the next several months leading to the [Battle of Jakku](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku"), Han Solo and Princess Leia prepared for the coming of their child. With Leia approaching labor, Solo hired a protocol droid named [T-2LC](/wiki/T-2LC "T-2LC") (or "Elsie") as a nanny. One day, Solo bought his wife a sack of [jogan fruits](/wiki/Jogan_fruit "Jogan fruit"). Leia was annoyed with Solo for overdoing it and reminded him that Dr. [Harter Kalonia](/wiki/Harter_Kalonia "Harter Kalonia") had said to incorporate jogan into her diet and not to replace everything with it. While chatting with his wife about the liberation of Kashyyyk and galactic politics, Han and Leia were contacted on [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram") by the New Republic operative Norra Wexley. Norra said that she was traveling to the [Inner Rim](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories") world of [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku") to hunt down Grand Admiral [Rae Sloane](/wiki/Rae_Sloane "Rae Sloane"), the purported instigator behind the Liberation Day attacks on Chandrila.[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

[Norra Wexley's team](/wiki/Norra_Wexley%27s_team "Norra Wexley's team") subsequently discovered that most of the Galactic Empire had retreated to Jakku. While Norra, the bounty hunter Jas Emari, and the battle droid Mister Bones infiltrated Jakku, Temmin and Sinjir returned to Chandrila with news about the Imperial presence. They visited Leia's domicile and warned Princess Leia and Han Solo about the Empire. Temmin tried to convince Solo to lend him his famous freighter, the *Millennium Falcon*. However, Solo thought that the mission was too risky and was unwilling to risk his ship.[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

Before the argument could escalate, Chancellor Mon Mothma entered the domicile and asked Temmin and Sinjir about the Imperial presence on Jakku. Following the meeting, Temmin and Sinjir managed to convince Han and Leia to lend them the *Millennium Falcon*. However, the two were stopped from leaving Chandrila by [Senate Guards](/wiki/Senate_Guard_(New_Republic) "Senate Guard (New Republic)") who had been dispatched by Senator [Tolwar Wartol](/wiki/Tolwar_Wartol "Tolwar Wartol"), a rival of Chancellor Mothma. Wartol had secretly installed a listening device inside T-2LC. In an attempt to discredit Chancellor Mothma, Wartol leaked news about the Imperial presence to [HoloNet News](/wiki/HoloNet_News "HoloNet News"). Solo and Leia learned about the leak while watching the morning news.[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

#### Unmasking a conspiracy[]

Han and Leia were later confronted by an angry Sinjir, who believed that they had double-crossed him and Temmin. Han and Leia managed to set the record straight. They then realized that Senator Wartol's leak and the Senate guards stopping Sinjir and Temmin were linked. When Sinjir voiced his suspicion that there was a spy bug in Leia's domicile, Han did not believe it, but Leia shared Sinjir's suspicion. Sinjir brought his former lover [Conder Kyl](/wiki/Conder_Kyl "Conder Kyl"), a slicer, to Leia's domicile. Conder found that the listening device was inside T-2LC. Following the discovery, Han told Elsie to hold still and warned that it was going to sting a little.[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

After removing the listening device and handing it to Chancellor Mothma, Han led a team consisting of Sinjir, Temmin, Conder, and Jom Barell to the New Republic's new capital of [Nakadia](/wiki/Nakadia "Nakadia"). Their [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Nakadia "Mission to Nakadia") was to investigate the five senators who had opposed Chancellor Mothma's resolution to send military forces to Jakku: [Ashmin Ek](/wiki/Ashmin_Ek "Ashmin Ek"), [Rethalow](/wiki/Rethalow "Rethalow"), [Dor Wieedo](/wiki/Dor_Wieedo "Dor Wieedo"), [Grelka Sorka](/wiki/Grelka_Sorka "Grelka Sorka"), and [Nim Tar](/wiki/Nim_Tar "Nim Tar"). While Sinjir and the others trailed four of the senators at a restaurant called [Izzik's](/wiki/Izzik%27s "Izzik's") in Nakadia's capital [Quarrow](/wiki/Quarrow "Quarrow"), Han went to spy on Senator Dor Wieedo. The Rodian senator was aboard his ship at the northernmost spaceport outside Quarrow.[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

After several hours had passed, Solo witnessed two [Nikto](/wiki/Nikto "Nikto") and a [Klatooinian](/wiki/Klatooinian "Klatooinian") approach Wieedo's ship. Unknown to Solo, these aliens were members of the [Red Key Raiders](/wiki/Red_Key_Raiders "Red Key Raiders"), a crime syndicate that was plotting with Black Sun to prolong the war. Solo managed to warn his comrades. However, the criminals discovered his presence and locked him in a rubbish bin. Meanwhile, Conder was kidnapped by other Red Key gangsters. Sinjir and Temmin found Solo and returned to the *Falcon*. Despite their setbacks, Jom managed to kidnap Senator Rethalow, who confessed to his dealings with Red Key and Black Sun.[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

Before they could spirit Rethalow away into hiding, Han and his team members decided to rescue Conder, [Nim Tar's child](/wiki/Nim_Tar%27s_child "Nim Tar's child"), and Sorka's [pet](/wiki/Grelka_Sorka%27s_jerba "Grelka Sorka's jerba") [jerba](/wiki/Jerba "Jerba"). Conder used his [transceiver tooth](/wiki/Transceiver_tooth "Transceiver tooth") to transmit his coordinates to Sinjir. Han and his team flew the *Millennium Falcon* through a red warehouse roof, which turned out to be the Red Key's base. After subduing the gangsters, they rescued Conder and Nim Tar's child. Posing as an adviser to the Chancellor, Sinjir transmitted a missive offering the five senators pardons and other political favors if they changed their votes during the re-vote scheduled to be held at the [Quarrow Senate house](/wiki/Quarrow_Senate_house "Quarrow Senate house"). As a result, Mothma's resolution passed, and the New Republic was able to dispatch military forces to Jakku.[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

#### War's end[]

:   "*Yeah. You, me, Luke. Chewie. The* Falcon*. Those two walking talking garbage cans. It feels weird we're not part of it.*"  
    "*We've got our own adventure.*"
:   ―Han and Leia[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

Following the events on Nakadia, Han returned home and reunited with his wife. When Leia praised him for "making things right", Solo told her that the Battle of Jakku was happening. He predicted that it would be a big battle. In private, Han confided that it felt strange that he, Leia, Luke, Chewbacca, C-3PO, and R2-D2 were not part of the final battle. Leia reassured him that they had their own adventure. Han responded that it was the end of an era while Leia replied that it was the start of a new one.[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

The Battle of Jakku turned out to be a decisive victory for the New Republic. Facing imminent defeat, [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier") [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda") on Coruscant sent peace overtures to Chancellor Mothma. Han and his wife attended the peace talks where Chancellor Mothma and Grand Vizier Amedda signed the [Imperial Instruments of Surrender](/wiki/Imperial_Instruments_of_Surrender "Imperial Instruments of Surrender") and the [Galactic Concordance](/wiki/Galactic_Concordance "Galactic Concordance"). The signing occurred during the third hour of Leia's labor, but she only told her husband after the ceremony was complete. Solo rushed her to the birthing chamber in the heart of [Hanna City](/wiki/Hanna_City "Hanna City").[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

 [![Solo with his wife and son](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/Han_Leia_and_Ben.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210085037) [![Solo with his wife and son](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/Han_Leia_and_Ben.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20161210085037)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/Han_Leia_and_Ben.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210085037) 

Solo with his wife and son

 

Leia gave birth to a son named Ben Solo. Following a gathering of family and friends, Han stared into his son's eyes and pondered how he had become a father. While Leia was showering in the next room, Solo told his son that while the whole galaxy was against them, they would still make it through okay. Though Solo confided that he might not make a good father, he promised to keep them pointed in the right direction. Solo also gave Ben his first lesson: sometimes doing the right thing doesn't mean following a straight line. Solo told his baby son not to tell his mother.[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

When Ben cried, Han tried to comfort him with a small [tooka doll](/wiki/Tooka_doll "Tooka doll"), but this failed to pacify the baby. Leia then heard her son crying. When Han said that it was not his fault, Leia reassured him that babies cried. Han sensed that Leia had a connection through the Force that he could never have with Ben. Han suggested using the Force, but Leia advised him to pick up their son and snuggle him. Han reluctantly snuggled his son and Ben stopped crying. When Han sighed that he could never have the same Force connection, Leia told him that fathers had a special connection with their offspring.[[159]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-159)

#### Fighting the Zantarrk Gang[]

:   "*You Heard the bounty hunter. Nobody's dying today.*"
:   ―Han Solo[[160]](#cite_note-SW_2025_1-160)

 [![Solo and Valance fought against the Zantarrk Gang.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/SoloValance-2025StarWars1.png/revision/latest?cb=20250524051602) [![Solo and Valance fought against the Zantarrk Gang.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/SoloValance-2025StarWars1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250524051602)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/SoloValance-2025StarWars1.png/revision/latest?cb=20250524051602) 

Solo and Valance fought against the Zantarrk Gang.

 

Around [6 ABY](/wiki/6_ABY "6 ABY"),[[161]](#cite_note-SW_25_Date-161) Solo was a in [Alshuey Town](/wiki/Alshuey_Town "Alshuey Town") on [Guat'a](/wiki/Guat%27a "Guat'a"). There, he helped Valance after was thrown out of a bar by the [Zantarrk Gang](/wiki/Zantarrk_Gang "Zantarrk Gang"). Solo sent out a warning shot against the gang members and saved Valance. The two of them then fought the Zantarrk in a gun fight. After dealing with the Zantarrk, Valance went with Solo to the *Millennium Falcon*.[[160]](#cite_note-SW_2025_1-160)

#### Baylan Skoll's gauntlet[]

Around [9 ABY](/wiki/9_ABY "9 ABY"),[[162]](#cite_note-Ahsoka_Date-162) during the search for [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Thrawn](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo"), the former Jedi Knight and [General](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") turned mercenary [Baylan Skoll](/wiki/Baylan_Skoll "Baylan Skoll") listed Solo's name in a device on his gauntlet, as well as the names of other key members of the [Heroes of Yavin](/wiki/Heroes_of_Yavin "Heroes of Yavin").[[163]](#cite_note-Part_Six-163)

#### Starting a family[]

:   "*I'll be back. We're not done, you and I. We'll see each other again. I'm gonna be a father and no way my kid won't have you in his life.*"
:   ―Han Solo parting ways with Chewbacca[[31]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-31)

Finding himself husband of an important politician, Han passed the time by becoming a successful racing pilot.[[164]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-164) On one occasion he returned to Corellia to compete in [The Gauntlet](/wiki/The_Gauntlet "The Gauntlet"), where he raced against [Greer Sonnel](/wiki/Greer_Sonnel "Greer Sonnel") and offered her a spot on his team for the [Five Sabers](/wiki/Five_Sabers "Five Sabers") race.[[165]](#cite_note-Scorched-165)

In the years after the end of the Galactic Civil War, Solo became the owner of a [shipping company](/wiki/Han_Solo%27s_shipping_company "Han Solo's shipping company") and developed a reputation for being a vigilant and responsible owner. Outside of his work, Han often raced for charity and sponsored several piloting matches. Due to his work, Solo found himself traveling through different systems, working on ships.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

Their son, Ben, proved to be Force-sensitive and was sent to be trained by his uncle Luke Skywalker in the ways of the Force.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-4) Meanwhile, his wife Leia served as a prominent [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") in the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate") on [Hosnian Prime](/wiki/Hosnian_Prime "Hosnian Prime"), the capital of the New Republic. Han and his family lived separate lives but he kept in touch with his wife via hologram.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

#### Working toward someday[]

:   "*You really think you'd enjoy the life of a racer? Bouncing around from one system to the next, working on ships, never knowing where you're headed next?*"  
    "*Doesn't sound that different from being a member of the Rebel Alliance.*"
:   ―Han and Leia talking about their plans to travel the galaxy together[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

 [![For a time, Solo managed the Five Sabers racing championship.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/Scorched-Han-Solo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170228025042) [![For a time, Solo managed the Five Sabers racing championship.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/Scorched-Han-Solo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20170228025042)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/Scorched-Han-Solo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170228025042) 

For a time, Solo managed the Five Sabers racing championship.

 

Twenty-four years after the Battle of Endor, Han Solo traveled to the planet [Theron](/wiki/Theron "Theron") to manage a prestigious racing championship called the Five Sabers. While staying in temporary quarters, he corresponded with Leia, who told her husband about the fractured state of the Galactic Senate. When Leia told Han about her desire to resign from the Senate, Han expressed puzzlement, since his wife had devoted much of her adult life to politics. Sensing Leia's frustration, Solo invited his wife to take a break and travel around the galaxy with him for three months. Despite their different personalities, Leia agreed that she needed a break from her senatorial career.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

However, Leia was forced to suspend her vacation plans after her faction, the [Populists](/wiki/Populists "Populists"), convinced her to stand for the position of [First Senator](/wiki/First_Senator "First Senator"). The rival [Centrist](/wiki/Centrists "Centrists") faction, which supported a stronger central government, had successfully passed a motion calling for the creation of First Senator in order to end the deadlock plaguing the Republic. Despite their initial opposition, the Populists, who preferred a more decentralized government, had decided to change tactics in order to prevent a Centrist from holding that office. Due to her prestige as a prominent former rebel leader, Leia had reluctantly agreed to allow an exploratory committee to explore her suitability for First Senator.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

While Han was repairing the rear engines of a starship, he was contacted by his wife. Solo was mildly disappointed with his wife's change of plans but agreed that a Populist should serve as First Senator. Solo also informed his wife that he was supervising the lunar relays of the Five Sabers. Due to the complicated nature of the repairs, Han remarked that he wished that Greer Sonnel, a former racer and [Junior Sabers](/wiki/Junior_Sabers "Junior Sabers") champion who was serving as Leia's pilot, was still on his team. When Leia apologized for delaying their planned holiday, Han reassured her that she was doing the right thing by putting duty to the New Republic first. Leia promised to take a break with her husband "someday."[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

In addition to the First Senatorship, Leia was involved in a sensitive Senate investigation into the Nikto crime lord [Rinnrivin Di](/wiki/Rinnrivin_Di "Rinnrivin Di")'s [cartel](/wiki/Rinnrivin_Di%27s_cartel "Rinnrivin Di's cartel"), a new criminal outfit that was choking the economy of the [Gaulus sector](/wiki/Gaulus_sector "Gaulus sector"). Leia was assisted in this investigation by an unlikely ally, the idealistic Centrist senator [Ransolm Casterfo](/wiki/Ransolm_Casterfo "Ransolm Casterfo"). Over the course of their investigation, the two discovered that Rinnrivin was linked to a paramilitary faction called the [Amaxine warriors](/wiki/Amaxine_warriors_(New_Republic_Era) "Amaxine warriors (New Republic Era)"). In an attempt to sow discord, [Arliz Hadrassian](/wiki/Arliz_Hadrassian "Arliz Hadrassian"), a former TIE fighter pilot who had become the Amaxines' leader, [bombed](/wiki/Napkin_Bombing "Napkin Bombing") the [New Republic senatorial complex](/wiki/New_Republic_senatorial_complex "New Republic senatorial complex")'s [conference building](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate_conference_building "New Republic Senate conference building"). Leia survived the bombing and transmitted a voice-message telling her husband that she was safe and that he did not need to come to Hosnian Prime. While on Theron, Solo received news about the Senate bombing and saw footage of the damage. Later, Solo contacted Leia to send his wife a goodwill message and to keep in touch.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

While Leia was visiting [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth") as part of her investigation, Han Solo sent a holomessage expressing hope that his wife's side project was going well. He informed her that the Five Sabers was heading to the fourth stage of the Sabers. Due to the sublight relay round, Han told her that he would be out of comm range for a while. He also told her to take care of herself and complimented her.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

#### Rescue on Sibensko[]

:   "*Sorry, I'm late, sweetheart.*"  
    "*Honey, you're right on time.*"
:   ―Han reuniting with his wife on Sibensko[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

Han and Leia would cross paths again due to unforeseen circumstances. Later, the Centrist Senator Lady [Carise Sindian](/wiki/Carise_Sindian "Carise Sindian"), a secret agent of an Imperial remnant known as the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order"), discovered information about Leia's true parentage as the daughter of Darth Vader on [Birren](/wiki/Birren "Birren"). Alarmed at the friendship between Ransolm Casterfo and Leia, Lady Carise shared this information with him, knowing Ransolm's hatred for Vader. Feeling betrayed, Casterfo upstaged the Senate hearing into Leia's nomination for First Senator by revealing Leia's parentage to the assembled senators. This revelation destroyed Leia's credibility and forced her to withdraw her nomination.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

Still determined to continue her investigation into Rinnrivin's cartel and the Amaxines, Leia and her team took leave to travel to [Sibensko](/wiki/Sibensko "Sibensko"), where the two groups were hiding. There, Leia discovered that the Amaxines were funding Rinnrivin's cartel and were also marshaling troops, weapons, and starships for an attack on the New Republic. During her [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Sibensko "Mission to Sibensko"), Leia was pursued by the Amaxine warriors and fled up a landing platform, where she was corned by two Amaxine starfighters. Han arrived on a [racer](/wiki/Racing_starfighter "Racing starfighter") and rescued his wife. Together, the couple shot down the enemy fighters. One of the fighters, a [B-wing](/wiki/A/SF-01_B-wing_starfighter "A/SF-01 B-wing starfighter"), collided with the underwater base's ammunition depot, triggering a massive explosion that destroyed the underwater city and the Amaxine army.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

Following the Sibensko mission, Han and his wife returned to Leia's apartment in Hosnian Prime. When Leia expressed despair that many of her former colleagues and comrades were shunning her for simply being Vader's daughter, Solo reassured her that this storm would pass and that people would remember her for who she was. Han counseled his wife to remember those friends who stuck by her and to ignore the rest of the galaxy. When Han criticized Casterfo, Leia sprung to her former friend's defense by pointing out that he was a decent man who hated Vader. Han then advised his wife to forget Casterfo and to use the political scandal as an opportunity to retire from politics for good.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

However, Leia still had one piece of unfinished business left: the findings of her investigation into Rinnrivin Di's cartel and the Amaxines. Leia wanted to address the Senate, but she needed to gain a quorum from a majority of senators. While Han thought that no more threats to the Republic existed with the demise of Rinnrivin and the Amaxines, Leia suspected that there were other like-minded groups seeking to overthrow the Republic. Han counseled his wife to rest for the night, and the couple expressed their love for each other.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

The following morning, the sports channels reported that Han Solo had left the [Theron system](/wiki/Theron_system "Theron system") after the end of the last Sabers round. There was also speculation on whether he would return for the final championship race. Later that evening, Han bought his wife [Bilbringi](/wiki/Bilbringi "Bilbringi") cheesy meat pies for dinner. While eating, the couple received news that Leia had received a quorum to address the Senate due to Casterfo's favorable vote. Han then told his wife that things would improve and that he would stay with her for as long as she needed him. Leia reassured her husband that she would be able to handle the hearing on her own and told him that he could return to the Sabers championship. Shortly, Solo returned to the Five Sabers race.[[19]](#cite_note-Bloodline-19)

### Cold War[]

#### Family strife[]

:   "*And Solo… Did you know that's not even his real name? He's a* lie*.*"
:   ―Ben Solo, to Snoke, about his father[[166]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-166)

At some point after the public revelations about Leia and Ben's relationship to Darth Vader,[[167]](#cite_note-Kylo_didn't_know_he_was_Vader's_heir-167) Han's son, Ben Solo, was seduced by [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke") and eventually succumbed to the dark side, [killing](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple") the Jedi Luke was [training](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"). Taking the blame for Ben's fall, Luke [exiled himself](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To"). Unable to cope with the loss of their son, Han and Leia separated.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-4)

Han and Chewbacca went back to being smugglers, which Han claimed was "the only thing he was ever good at." Meanwhile, Leia became the leader of the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance"), a paramilitary organization aimed at fighting the First Order, which had begun to pose a threat to the New Republic. Han then got himself into a lot of debt with various creditors including the notorious [Guavian Death Gang](/wiki/Guavian_Death_Gang "Guavian Death Gang") and [Kanjiklub](/wiki/Kanjiklub "Kanjiklub").

#### Losing the *Falcon*[]

:   "*Short-handed? I can help. I can be your co-pilot.*"
:   ―Gannis Ducain to Han Solo[[168]](#cite_note-Adventures_18-168)

In [31 ABY](/wiki/31_ABY "31 ABY")[[169]](#cite_note-Date1-169) Solo traveled to Maz's castle, where he spoke with Kanata about Chewbacca being unable to do a job with him. [Gannis Ducain](/wiki/Gannis_Ducain "Gannis Ducain"), who worked for Kanata, overheard and suggested he help on the job. The job was to deliver cargo to [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis "Christophsis"). When Han and Ducain arrived, Han left Ducain to guard the *Millennium Falcon* whilst he met with his contact. Ducain, however, stole *Falcon*. Ducain became a rich [gunrunner](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler"). One day the [Irving Boys](/wiki/Irving_Boys "Irving Boys") stole the *Falcon* from him.[[168]](#cite_note-Adventures_18-168)

After losing the *Falcon*, Han and Chewbacca obtained a [*Baleen*-class heavy freighter](/wiki/Baleen-class_heavy_freighter "Baleen-class heavy freighter") named the *[Eravana](/wiki/Eravana "Eravana")* that they used for their smuggling operations and even assembled a crew to assist them. Han spent the majority of his free time trying to track down the *Falcon*.[[4]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-4)

#### Smuggler's run[]

 [![Confrontation with bounty hunters in the Serendipity](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/Team_Falcon_in_Seredipity_cantina.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160914041503) [![Confrontation with bounty hunters in the Serendipity](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/Team_Falcon_in_Seredipity_cantina.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20160914041503)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/Team_Falcon_in_Seredipity_cantina.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160914041503) 

Confrontation with bounty hunters in the *Serendipity*

 

Sometime later, Solo and Chewbacca went to the *Serendipity*, a yacht that was owned by Leighton. There, Solo engaged a trio of bounty hunters—[Strater](/wiki/Strater "Strater"), [Hove](/wiki/Hove "Hove"), and [Rigger](/wiki/Rigger "Rigger")—sent to capture him on the *Serendipity* cantina, and told them about their mission to Cyrkon before they realized who he was. Once they were aware of Solo's identity, Chewbacca snuck behind them and took hold of Rigger, only to send him flying to the *Serendipity*'s door and knock Strater out with a punch, while Solo disarmed Bobbie. Then, the Corellian told them to warn their possible employers (Ducain, the Irving Boys, the Guavians, etc.) that they were not afraid of them, before saying goodbye to Leighton and leaving the bar together.[[34]](#cite_note-Smuggler's_Run-34)

#### Alderaanian data archive heist[]

 [![Solo, posing as a First Order officer aboard ](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/SoloChewbacca-PoeDameronAnnual2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180902200518) [![Solo, posing as a First Order officer aboard ](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/SoloChewbacca-PoeDameronAnnual2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20180902200518)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/SoloChewbacca-PoeDameronAnnual2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180902200518) 

Solo, posing as a First Order officer aboard [Mek Nu'Tiv's cruiser](/wiki/Mek_Nu%27Tiv%27s_cruiser "Mek Nu'Tiv's cruiser")

 

Solo and Chewbacca stole a [*Xi*-class light shuttle](/wiki/Xi-class_light_shuttle "Xi-class light shuttle") from the [shipyard](/wiki/Fluzhi_Clan_Shipyard "Fluzhi Clan Shipyard") of the [Fluzhi Clan](/wiki/Fluzhi_Clan "Fluzhi Clan"). They escaped from the shipyard and planned to use codes from [Finwej](/wiki/Finwej "Finwej") to steal a weapons archive from [Mek Nu'Tiv](/wiki/Mek_Nu%27Tiv "Mek Nu'Tiv").
